The 3 multi-user surfaces are the real child-safety wins; the 2 private ones are standard-consistency. **$0** (free moderations endpoint + cache). **Migration:** none. **iOS:** server-side shared routes; iOS inherits. tsc clean.

- fix(economy): **Arena settlement through the RPC + 5 ledger-integrity fixes (multi-agent discovery batch 1)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; no migration). A six-lens adversarial discovery sweep surfaced these, each verified against the real code. **(1) CRITICAL — arena/complete** was the one PvP path still doing a raw read-modify-write on `coins` (the exact bug class fixed everywhere else; arena was never swept). Refactored to the atomic `update_user_coins` RPC: winner credited `+wager` cashable, loser debited `-min(wager, balance)` cashable (clamped from the read like settle.ts; `cashable` NOT `spend` so a wager loss doesn't inflate `lifetime_fangs_spent`). ELO/win-loss counters stay a separate raw write. **(2) shop/purchase refund** used `cashable` instead of `spend_refund`, so a refunded purchase left `lifetime_fangs_spent` inflated (corrupting the V2 cash-out gate). **(3-5) save-quiz-results** credited the consecutive-quiz bonus, streak-milestone bonus, and bet payout via RPCs whose error was never checked — a silent credit failure still wrote a phantom `coin_transactions` audit row and reported the reward as earned. Now each checks the RPC error before logging/claiming (bonus zeroes out, milestone skips, bet logs LOUDLY for reconciliation since it's post-claim). **(6) claim-bounty** XP write + **(7) streak-revive** audit insert now check/await their errors instead of dropping them. **Migration:** none. **iOS:** server-side shared routes; iOS inherits. tsc clean. (Streak-milestone double-credit RACE and arena-queue index are separate migration-needing items, batched next.)

- fix(economy): **Record competitive Fang movements in coin_transactions (audit-trail gap)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; no migration). Competitive PvP settlement recorded each player's Fang delta only on the `competitive_matches.fang_delta` jsonb — so wins/losses never appeared in `coin_transactions`, leaving them out of the user's Fang history and any ledger sum. `settleClaimedMatch` now writes a best-effort `competitive_match` audit row (signed `amount = effectiveDelta`, `reference_id = match.id`, description `Competitive win|loss|draw (<mode>)`) alongside the atomic coin write. Safe + non-double-counting: settlement runs exactly once per match (the active->completing claim gates it), the loss-cap reads competitive deltas from `fang_delta` (NOT coin_transactions, verified), and `coin_transactions.type` has no CHECK constraint so the new type needs no migration. A failed log never claws back the settled balance. **Migration:** none. **iOS:** server-side; inherits it. tsc clean.

- feat(safety): **Extend UGC moderation to DMs, lobby chat, and Bluff fake answers (the #8 follow-up)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; no migration; $0). The earlier moderation pass wired `moderateText` into bank names + usernames but left the live chat surfaces raw. Now the three user-to-user text surfaces that broadcast to OTHER users run through the same gate before persist/broadcast: **DMs** (`/api/social/messages` POST — private but still a direct-harassment vector on a 13+ app), **party lobby chat** (`/api/party/rooms/[code]/lobby-chat` — fans out live to every room member), **Bluff fake answers** (`/api/party/bluff/rounds/[id]/answer` — every player sees the decoy in the guess phase; forfeit-marker constants are skipped), and **party room names** (`/api/party/rooms` POST `display_name` — surfaces in the join/discovery flow). Each blocks with a friendly message + writes a `flagged_content` audit row (surfaces `dm` / `lobby_chat` / `bluff_answer` / `room_name`) and inherits `moderateText`'s denylist floor + free OpenAI-moderations layer + fail-safe. Verified NOT needed elsewhere in party: trivia answers are server-sourced MCQ `choice_index` values, not free text. **$0** (moderations endpoint is free + cached). **Migration:** none. **iOS:** server-side on shared routes; iOS chat inherits it. tsc clean.

- fix(security): **Lock down 9 server-only SECURITY DEFINER functions + pin 6 mutable search_paths (migration 076, APPLIED 2026-06-14)** (web; committed + applied 2026-06-14). A Supabase database-linter audit (security advisors) surfaced two real hardening gaps. **(A) Public RPC on privileged functions:** 9 SECURITY DEFINER functions — `grant_polyglot_badge`, `grant_knowledge_sharer_badge`, `grant_streak_emblem`, `grant_mastery_medal`, `reap_afk_presence`, `set_active_session`, `clear_active_session`, `ping_presence`, `guard_profile_equipped` — were EXECUTE-able by `anon`/`authenticated` via `/rest/v1/rpc/<fn>`. All are called EXCLUSIVELY server-side via the service-role client (verified: cosmetic-grants + mastery/login-bonus routes, lib/presence + heartbeat route, the reap cron, and a trigger), so a signed-in user could hit them directly and e.g. self-grant cosmetic badges, fire the AFK reaper, or spoof another user's presence. Migration 076 REVOKEs anon/authenticated EXECUTE (service role bypasses grants, so the app is unaffected). **(B) Mutable search_path:** pinned `search_path = public` on `calc_level_from_xp`, `class_assignments_touch_updated_at`, `on_profile_xp_change`, `handle_new_user`, `vocab_banks_derive_slug`, `vocab_words_touch_updated_at` (additive GUC, no body/logic change). `current_app_role` / `clone_bank` / `weekly_quiz_leaderboard` deliberately left (may be intentionally client-callable — separate verified pass). **APPLIED 2026-06-14** (after Sam's go); verified anon/authenticated EXECUTE is now false on all 9 (service_role retains it) and all 6 search_paths are pinned. A follow-up `076b` revoked `guard_profile_equipped` from PUBLIC too (a trigger fn whose grant was held via the implicit PUBLIC role). **Also flagged (Sam, dashboard-only):** enable Auth "Leaked Password Protection" (HaveIBeenPwned) in the Supabase Auth settings. The `rls_enabled_no_policy` INFOs (ai_call_log, flagged_content, game_rewards, reward_claims, stripe_webhook_events, etc.) are INTENTIONAL — those are service-role-only tables where RLS-on + no-policy = deny-all is the correct lockdown. **Migration:** 076, READY/unapplied. tsc N/A (SQL).

- fix(security): **Move all Fang-earning routes into the 60/min anti-burst rate-limit bucket** (web; committed 2026-06-14; no migration). Six currency-mutating EARN routes (`missions/claim`, `focus-session`, `daily-drill/complete`, `spin/roll`, `login-bonus`, `mastery/sessions/[id]/complete`) sat only in the loose 100/min catch-all, while every other Fang-mutating route (save-quiz-results, place-bet, claim-bounty, games/reward, shop/*, ninny spend routes) was already in the tighter 60/min `fin` bucket. Each earn route now has its own server-side idempotency/daily cap (from the economy-integrity work), so this is the secondary IP-level anti-burst defense, but it should be uniform — added them to the `fin` test (the mastery one via a `/sessions/[id]/complete` regex). No legitimate flow approaches 60/min on these (all are a-few-times-a-day actions). **Migration:** none. **iOS:** middleware fronts the shared API; iOS inherits it. tsc clean.

- fix(economy): **Dual-ledger reconciliation backfill (migration 075, APPLIED 2026-06-14)** (web; committed + applied 2026-06-14). After the part-1/part-2 RPC sweep stopped FUTURE drift, an audit showed the ledger had ALREADY drifted: 8 of 17 profiles have `coins != fangs_cashable + fangs_iap`, +643 Fangs of `coins` untracked in any bucket (max 145 on one user), every drifted row with `iap=0` and POSITIVE drift — i.e. historical raw EARN writes that credited `coins` but never the cashable bucket. The V2 cash-out gate reads the bucket columns, so this would mis-price cash-out at launch. Migration 075 trues each row up so `coins = fangs_cashable + fangs_iap` again, **without changing `coins`** (the spendable balance the user sees is byte-identical; only the accounting split is corrected): `new_iap = least(old_iap, coins)`, `new_cashable = coins - new_iap` (preserves the audited IAP bucket, puts the untracked remainder in cashable; for the current iap=0 rows this is just `cashable = coins`). Idempotent + guarded to `coins >= 0`. **APPLIED 2026-06-14** (after Sam's go); verified 8 rows reconciled, 0 drift remaining, total coins unchanged (7572 == 7572). Pre-cash-out, so zero user-facing impact. **Migration:** 075, READY/unapplied. **iOS:** reads the same columns; inherits the corrected ledger. tsc N/A (SQL).

- fix(economy): **Competitive PvP settlement now uses the atomic RPC (dual-ledger integrity, part 2)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; no migration). `lib/competitive/settle.ts` (the single settlement core behind /complete, /forfeit, and the reap-stale cron) wrote every participant's Fang result with a raw `profiles.update({ coins })` coupled to the ELO column — so every settled match drifted `coins` away from `fangs_cashable` (the V2 cash-out ledger) and could lose a concurrent grant. Split into an atomic `update_user_coins` coin write + a plain ELO write. **Source choice matters here:** both a win (credit) and a loss (debit) use source `'cashable'`, NOT `'spend'`, because a wager loss must NOT inflate `lifetime_fangs_spent` (that's the 60%-spend cash-out gate — a loss isn't "spending"). Service role may pass a negative `'cashable'` delta and the RPC clamps cashable at 0; a rare concurrent balance drop surfaces as a logged P0001 and that one loss is skipped (never a crash or negative balance). The per-match `fang_delta` audit on `competitive_matches` and the loss-cap/engagement-void logic are unchanged. **Remaining (part 3, NOT done):** `lib/db.ts incrementCoins` + its callers (saveQuizSession, badge bonus, duel win) still raw-write. It can't be converted in place — `lib/db.ts` is imported by 13+ client components, so pulling in the service-role client/RPC there would risk bundling `SUPABASE_SECRET_KEY` into client JS. The correct fix is extracting the server-only grant functions into a separate module (and resolving the open question of how those anon-client cross-user credits behave under RLS today); flagged for a dedicated pass. **Migration:** none. **iOS:** server-side, shared route; iOS inherits it. tsc clean.

- fix(economy): **Route 9 more Fang earn/spend paths through the atomic RPC (dual-ledger integrity, part 1)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; no migration). Nine routes still mutated `profiles.coins` with a raw read-modify-write + a manual `coin_transactions` insert. Two problems with that: (1) a read-then-write can LOSE a concurrent grant (the classic lost-update race the RPC was built to kill), and (2) it bypasses the dual ledger, so `coins` drifts away from `fangs_cashable + fangs_iap` — silently corrupting the V2 cash-out accounting (the 60%-spend gate reads those columns). Converted **earns** (missions/claim, mastery/sessions/complete, focus-session, daily-drill/complete, party Sketchy letter-grant + `lib/party/sketch-fangs.awardSketchFangs`) to credit via `update_user_coins(..., 'cashable')` and **spends** (ninny/unlock, ninny/generate, ninny/abandon) to debit via `'spend'` with refunds via `'spend_refund'`. Each route's existing idempotency gate is preserved (the mission claim flip, the closed mastery session, the daily-drill completion row, the Sketchy unique-reason ledger) and the manual `coin_transactions` audit row stays (the RPC only writes the balance columns). ninny's old optimistic-concurrency deduct + read-then-rollback refund are gone — the RPC's `coins + delta >= 0` guard is the atomic check now (a lost race surfaces as a friendly 402, not a double-charge). **Deliberately deferred (part 2):** `lib/db.ts incrementCoins` (it runs on the ANON client, so it can't call the service-role RPC without risking a service-key bundle into client code — needs a server-only refactor first) and `lib/competitive/settle.ts` (a coupled multi-user coins+ELO write with loss-cap clamping — converting it safely needs its own pass). Both are flagged in the code-adjacent notes. **Migration:** none. **iOS:** server-side economy fix on shared routes; iOS inherits it. tsc clean.

- feat(growth): **Streak-at-risk re-engagement email (built, DORMANT)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; migration 074 applied; $0). A daily cron that emails users whose streak is ALIVE but about to lapse, the single highest-leverage retention nudge we don't yet send. `app/api/cron/streak-reminder` targets users whose `last_activity_at` was 24h-44h ago (so a quiz TODAY still ticks the streak per the 20h-48h increment window in save-quiz-results, with >= ~4h of runway before the 48h reset cliff) and `streak >= 2` (a 1-day streak isn't worth a panic email and would shadow the day-1 "you're cooking" mail). New `lib/emails/templates/streak-reminder.ts` (Ninny voice, "your N-day streak is on the line," registered in the index + the `/dev/emails` preview). Gated on the EMAIL toggle `notifications_email.streak_alert` (default ON; skip only if explicitly false), independent of the in-app card, mirroring academia-digest. **Idempotency:** migration 074 adds `profiles.streak_reminder_sent_at` + a partial index; a self-resetting gate sends only when the marker is older than `last_activity_at` and stamps `now()` AFTER a confirmed send (a failed send retries next run; a single streak-session yields at most one reminder even across many cron runs; studying again re-arms it). Auth/Resend/heartbeat/recipient-resolution copied verbatim from academia-digest (header-only Bearer CRON_SECRET, server-resolved recipient via `getUserById`, display-name HTML-escaped, `putCronHeartbeat("streak-reminder")`). **DORMANT:** intentionally NOT in `vercel.json` because it sends real email I can't eyeball autonomously. **Activation (Sam):** preview at `/dev/emails?template=streakReminder`, confirm RESEND/EMAIL_FROM/CRON_SECRET in prod, add the cron entry (suggested `0 21 * * *` = ~5pm ET so the nudge lands in the user's afternoon), redeploy; a manual Bearer GET smoke-tests one real run first. **Deferred (documented, not built):** a backward-looking "your week on Lionade" recap was scoped OUT this round because the existing academia-digest already owns the `weekly_report` toggle + the weekly channel, so a second weekly cron would double-email Academia users; the right design is folding a recap section into the one weekly email rather than bolting on a colliding cron, which is a refactor of a LIVE cron best done with Sam's eyes on the merged template. **Migration:** 074, applied. **iOS:** server-side email cron, no iOS surface (iOS streak nudges would be push via expo-notifications, a separate track). tsc clean.

- feat(safety): **Real UGC moderation on bank names + usernames (COPPA/legal)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; migration 073 applied; $0). `lib/moderation.isClean` (a denylist) was wired into exactly one place (bank RENAME) — bank CREATE and change-username published raw user text with no filter, so a slur-named public bank could surface in Discover and abusive handles went live. New `lib/moderation-ugc.ts` `moderateText` layers OpenAI's **free** `/v1/moderations` (omni-moderation-latest, 4s timeout, in-memory cache) on top of the denylist FLOOR: the denylist blocks the worst instantly + offline; the model catches context-dependent hate/harassment/sexual/self-harm a substring list can't. **Fail-safe:** on timeout/API error it falls back to the denylist verdict, so an OpenAI blip never blocks the app. Wired into bank-CREATE + change-username (block + a `flagged_content` audit row, migration 073). **$0** (the moderations endpoint is free, no token billing). **Follow-up:** DMs / lobby-chat / Bluff fake-answers can adopt `moderateText` next. **Migration:** 073, applied. tsc clean.

- fix(economy): **Refund ledger correctness + streak-revive rollback fix** (web; committed 2026-06-14; migration 072 applied). (1) **streak-revive could destroy the streak the user paid to revive:** on a claim-write failure the old path set `streak: 0, last_activity_at: null` (plus a stale raw `coins` rollback). Rewrote the flow — spend via the RPC, conditionally claim (`.eq('status','open').select()`, atomic so a concurrent double-spend refunds), then restore the streak LAST, so a failure can never nuke it and any post-spend failure refunds. (2) **Refunds over-credited cashable and never unwound `lifetime_fangs_spent`** (corrupting the V2 60%-spend cash-out gate). Migration 072 adds a `spend_refund` branch to `update_user_coins` (a strict superset of the existing RPC, every other branch byte-identical) that credits cashable and decrements `lifetime_fangs_spent`; place-bet's refund + streak-revive's rollbacks now use it. (Full per-spend cashable/iap proportion restoration is a V2 refinement, no user impact pre-cash-out.) **Migration:** 072, applied. tsc clean.

- perf(leaderboard): **Index the ELO ladders + bound the weekly leaderboard aggregation** (web; committed 2026-06-14; migration 071 applied). (1) `competitive_elo` and `squad_elo` (added in migration 054) had NO index, so every Competitive/Squad ladder open full-table-sorted profiles — added partial DESC indexes on the public set (plus arena_elo). (2) `getLeaderboard` fetched EVERY weekly `quiz_reward` coin_transactions row with no limit then aggregated in Node (a sequential scan growing with platform activity, on the dashboard hot path) — replaced with a partial `(created_at) WHERE type='quiz_reward'` index + a bounded `weekly_quiz_leaderboard` GROUP BY...LIMIT RPC. The visibility/opt-out filter + over-fetch are preserved, and it no longer streams all of coin_transactions to the client (a small privacy win). **Migration:** 071, applied. tsc clean.

- fix(economy): **Atomic daily-window claims for spin / login-bonus / place-bet** (web; committed 2026-06-14; migration 069 applied). All three were check-then-act, so two concurrent POSTs double-paid: spin minted up to 800F + a rare cosmetic twice, login-bonus the tiered+multiplied bonus twice, place-bet double-debited the stake and left two active bets. Migration 069 adds (1) a reusable atomic `claim_cooldown(user_id, kind, cooldown_seconds)` RPC, advisory-lock serialized so the window-check + insert is atomic, gating spin + login-bonus before they pay; and (2) a partial UNIQUE on `daily_bets(user_id) WHERE resolved_at IS NULL` so a user holds at most one active bet (the second concurrent insert fails 23505 and place-bet refunds the debit). login-bonus also moved off its raw `coins` read-modify-write (whose stale-coins rollback could clobber a concurrent balance change) to the atomic `update_user_coins` RPC. **Migration:** 069, applied. tsc clean.

- fix(payments): **Per-payment idempotency for Fang IAP credits (review follow-up to 068)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; migration 070 applied). The adversarial review of 068 found a residual: the 5-min stale-lock self-heal can re-run `handleFangIapPayment`, and `update_user_coins` has no per-payment dedup, so a slow-then-killed handler could double-credit a Fang pack. New `credit_fang_iap` RPC (migration 070) does the idempotency-gate insert (partial UNIQUE on the Stripe `session.id`) AND the iap credit in ONE transaction: a duplicate session conflicts and returns false without crediting, and a mid-function crash rolls back cleanly so a Stripe retry re-credits. The handler now calls it instead of a separate credit + best-effort log. **Migration:** 070, applied. tsc clean.

- fix(payments): **Stripe webhook concurrency claim (stop double-crediting Fang IAP)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; migration 068 applied). The webhook recorded its dedup row AFTER the handler ran and only short-circuited on status='processed', so two concurrent/overlapping Stripe deliveries both passed the read-only lookup and ran the handler twice (e.g. crediting a Fang pack twice for one payment). Now an atomic `claim_stripe_event` RPC (migration 068 adds a 'processing' status + the claim) makes exactly one delivery own the work: it INSERTs a 'processing' lock or re-claims a previously-'errored' / stale-'processing' one, returning claimed/duplicate/in_progress. The errored + stale-lock re-claim preserves Stripe's retry-a-failed-event behavior, and a crashed handler's lock self-heals after 5 minutes so the next retry re-processes. **Migration:** 068, applied. tsc clean.

- fix(economy): **save-quiz-results idempotency + atomic bet claim (core earn-path double-credit fixes)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; migration 067 applied). Two money bugs on the primary earn path. (1) The daily-bet resolution UPDATE was keyed only on the bet id with NO `resolved_at` guard, so two concurrent quiz submits each credited the payout (up to 5x stake, repeatedly); now a conditional claim `.eq(id).is('resolved_at', null).select()` lets only the first submit win and credit. (2) No replay protection — a retried POST re-credited up to 500 Fangs; a client-supplied per-attempt `attempt_id` + a partial UNIQUE(user_id, attempt_id) (migration 067) makes the INSERT the idempotency gate, returning the prior result on a replay without re-crediting. The client's `finishQuiz` sends a fresh uuid per attempt (genuine separate quizzes still each earn; the id is optional + back-compatible). **Migration:** 067, applied. **iOS:** server-side fix on the shared route; iOS quiz submits inherit it. tsc clean.

- fix(economy): **Cap the /api/games/reward Fang faucet (critical inflation fix)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; migration 066 applied to prod). The route credited Fangs on every POST with NO daily cap, NO idempotency, and a raw read-modify-write — a script could mint thousands of Fangs/min in a loop (discovery flagged it as the single largest uncontrolled inflation source). Now a new `game_rewards(user_id, game_type, reward_date)` claim table (migration 066) enforces ONE paid completion per score game (roardle/blitz/flashcards/timeline) per UTC day via an INSERT-first claim; the credit is atomic via `update_user_coins` (cashable bucket) instead of a raw write, so it can't lose updates or desync the dual ledger; and the dead, unprotected `pardy_correct` entry (a 200-Fang faucet that bypassed Pardy's own per-tile claims) is removed. Clients (`app/games/page.tsx`, `compete/blitz`) honor the server's actual `awarded` so the daily-cap UX stays truthful. Pardy unchanged (it already had per-tile idempotency in `/api/games/pardy/submit`). **Migration required:** 066, applied. **iOS:** server-side economy fix; iOS games hit the same route and inherit the cap (no iOS change). tsc clean.

- feat(infra): **AWS cost guardrails + remote Terraform state (roadmap steps 1-2)** (Terraform only; committed 2026-06-14; free; Sam runs `terraform apply`). **Step 1, cost guardrails:** `aws_budgets_budget` ($25/mo, forecast >80% + actual >100% email alerts to Sam) plus `aws_ce_anomaly_monitor` + `aws_ce_anomaly_subscription` (ML anomaly detection across the whole account, alerts on >= $10 anomalous spend) so a runaway bill (a Bedrock token loop, an idle endpoint, a CloudFront egress spike) pings Sam before it's a surprise. **Step 2, remote Terraform state:** `lionade-tf-state` S3 bucket (versioned, SSE-AES256, Block Public Access on, noncurrent-version lifecycle) + `lionade-tf-locks` DynamoDB table (PAY_PER_REQUEST, LockID), and `terraform/backend.tf` with the commented `backend "s3"` block + a bootstrap runbook (apply with local state first, then `terraform init -migrate-state`). Reviewed by a principal-SA pass (sound: modern anomaly `threshold_expression` form, canonical lock table, correct two-step bootstrap ordering). **Manual steps (Sam):** enable Cost Explorer once in the Billing console, toggle Free Tier usage alerts, `terraform apply`, then follow the state-migration runbook in `backend.tf`. **No IOS_PARITY row:** pure AWS infrastructure, no product or iOS surface. `terraform validate` + `fmt` clean.

- fix(privacy) + feat(infra): **GDPR storage-erasure fix (live) + S3 upload pilot Phase A (dormant)** (web; committed 2026-06-14; the GDPR fix is LIVE, the S3 pilot is DORMANT until activated; $0 today, S3 storage + egress flagged for go-live). **(1) GDPR Art. 17 fix (live).** Account deletion left user-uploaded files orphaned: the reaper's `auth.admin.deleteUser` cascades Postgres FK rows, but Supabase has no `auth.users -> storage.objects` cascade and a grep confirmed there was no `storage.remove()` anywhere. So a deleted user's `note-images` photos + `class-syllabi` PDFs survived deletion forever (verified against prod: 0 orphans today only because no uploader had deleted yet, so the leak was latent, now fixed before it could trigger). New `lib/storage-purge.ts` recursively lists + removes both owner-folder buckets; `app/api/cron/reap-pending-deletions` now purges BEFORE the cascade, **fail-closed** (a purge error skips the hard-delete so the account stays scheduled and retries, never orphaning PII). **(2) S3 upload pilot Phase A (dormant).** The web/infra half of moving `note-images` blobs to a private S3 bucket via presigned upload (spec `docs/specs/note-images-s3-pilot.md`): `lib/s3.ts` (presigned POST upload, ownership-checked presigned GET read, two-principal least-privilege clients, dormant-safe config guards), `POST /api/note-images/presign` + `GET /api/note-images/sign-read` (both 503 until configured), the dual-backend `getSignedNoteImageUrl` resolver (`note-images/` -> Supabase unchanged; `user-uploads/` -> S3), and `terraform/main.tf` (new `lionade-user-uploads` private bucket, Block Public Access on, SSE-AES256, versioned, CORS prod-origin-only, split IAM users). Ships SAFE: nothing writes S3 tokens until iOS Phase B + a manual `terraform apply` + Vercel env, so every S3 path is inert today. **Hardened via two adversarial review passes** (spec-level + implementation-level): equality ownership check (not startsWith), key == token (no remap), presigned-POST size + type + Content-Disposition, **fail-closed on the half-configured credential state** (live write path + missing reaper creds now throws rather than orphaning PII), recursive-purge type-cast guard, legacy-resolver shape guard. **Migration required:** No. **Manual steps to activate (Sam):** `terraform apply` (creates the bucket + IAM, emits 4 sensitive key outputs) -> set Vercel env (`AWS_REGION`, `USER_UPLOADS_BUCKET`, the web key pair, the reaper key pair) -> Privacy Policy edits (spec §8.5) -> iOS Phase B. **iOS:** Phase B (the upload swap) NOT built, tracked in `IOS_PARITY.md`; the GDPR fix already covers iOS uploads (same buckets, same reaper). **Chain:** dev-database verify -> dev-backend + ops-terraform -> security-auth-guardian + quality-code-reviewer + quality-qa-tester (two adversarial passes, 18 findings, all confirmed ones fixed) -> docs.

- feat(learn): **Photograph your syllabus, client-side OCR for Mastery Mode** (web-only; committed 2026-06-14; **$0, no API cost, no AWS Textract**). The Mastery create funnel (`/learn/mastery`) gained a "Scan a photo of your syllabus" button beside the textarea. A photo, screenshot, or scan is OCR'd **entirely in the browser** with tesseract.js (WebAssembly), and the recognized text is dropped into the SAME textarea that already feeds `POST /api/mastery/parse`, so the parse / AI pipeline is unchanged, it just gains a second input mode. **Why not Textract:** AWS Textract is free for only 1,000 pages/month for 3 months then bills ~$1.50/1k pages, so it fails the "must cost nothing" bar; client-side OCR is genuinely $0 with no per-use charge. **Engine hosting:** tesseract.js@7 (worker + SIMD-LSTM core + the English model, ~17 MB) is **self-hosted under `/public/tess` and loaded same-origin**, so it rides the existing tight CSP (`default-src 'self'`, `script-src 'self' 'unsafe-eval'`, `connect-src 'self'`) with NO widening and no third-party CDN dependency. The model downloads once and the browser caches it; the photo bytes never leave the device. **Component:** new `components/Mastery/PhotoImport.tsx`, lazy-imported so the WASM never lands in the initial bundle. **Reviewed** via a 4-lens adversarial pass (code / QA / a11y / cost-claim, 13 findings fixed): HEIC/HEIF rejected up front with export-to-JPG guidance, 10 MB size cap, 90s timeout, one-time-download progress percentage, a persistent focusable trigger (focus never lost mid-scan), a single non-spammy `aria-live` status covering terminal states, and a `motion-safe` spinner. **Migration required:** No. **Breaking changes:** None. **iOS:** NOT built, tracked as a real gap in `IOS_PARITY.md` (the port would use on-device Apple Vision / ML Kit, also $0). **Chain:** dev-frontend -> 4-lens review (quality-code-reviewer + quality-qa-tester + design-accessibility + security-auditor) with adversarial verification -> docs. **Verification:** typecheck clean, route compiles, all engine assets serve 200 same-origin; the actual in-browser scan is pending a manual device check.

- feat(admin): **Admin Pro/Platinum grants — time-boxed, revocable, audited entitlements** (web-only; shipped 2026-06-14; zero AI cost). Until now the only paths to a paid tier were a live Stripe subscription or Sam bumping `profiles.plan` by hand, which left no record of who granted it, why, whether it should expire, or how to revoke it without clobbering a real Stripe tier. This makes manual / comped / promo / support entitlements first-class and auditable WITHOUT changing any effective-plan reader. **(1) New `plan_grants` table + resolver.** Migration `065_plan_grants.sql` adds `plan_grants` (`user_id`, `tier` pro|platinum, `expires_at` nullable = lifetime, `source` default 'admin', `granted_by`, `reason`, `revoked_at` soft-revoke, `created_at`) with a per-user index and a not-revoked partial index. `profiles.plan` stays the single EFFECTIVE plan every existing reader trusts (`lib/use-plan.ts` `isPaid`, `lib/mastery-plan.ts` `effectiveTier`, save-quiz-results, missions, competitive); none of those readers change. New `lib/plan-grants.ts` `recomputeEffectivePlan(userId)` is the one write path that folds two sources into `profiles.plan`: `effective = highest of [ stripe_baseline , highest ACTIVE grant tier ]` where `stripe_baseline = (subscription_status === 'active') ? subscription_tier : 'free'`, an active grant is `revoked_at IS NULL AND (expires_at IS NULL OR expires_at > now())`, and tier order is platinum > pro > free. It writes only on change and is idempotent. **(2) Admin UI.** New `components/admin/SubscriptionGrantCard.tsx` on `/admin/users/[id]` shows the effective plan + any active grant (tier, expiry, reason, source, who issued it) and lets staff grant Pro/Platinum for 1 month / 3 months / 6 months / 1 year / Lifetime with an optional logged reason, or revoke the active grant. **(3) Backend routes.** `POST /api/admin/users/[id]/grant-plan` (admin only, validates tier + `durationDays` 1..10000 or null for lifetime, inserts the grant then recomputes) and `POST /api/admin/users/[id]/revoke-plan` (admin only, soft-revokes every active grant then recomputes); both write `plan_grant` / `plan_revoke` to `admin_audit_log` with `granted_by` = the acting staff id. `GET /api/admin/users/[id]/grant-plan` returns the current active grant for the card. **(4) Stripe webhook respects grants.** `app/api/stripe/webhook/route.ts` no longer force-writes `profiles.plan`; it writes only the Stripe baseline columns then calls `recomputeEffectivePlan`, so a Stripe event (including `subscription.deleted` and a flip to `past_due`) never downgrades a user who still holds an active admin grant, and a higher real Stripe tier still wins. **(5) Expiry cron.** New `GET /api/cron/expire-grants` (CRON_SECRET bearer auth, daily in `vercel.json`) finds users whose only grant lapsed overnight and recomputes them so a cached elevated `profiles.plan` drops to baseline. **Security:** `plan_grants` is RLS-on with a SELECT-own policy and NO write policy, so users can read their own grants but cannot self-grant; all writes go through the service role in the admin routes. **Migration required:** Yes, `lib/migrations/065_plan_grants.sql`, **applied to production 2026-06-14.** Three client/route contract bugs from the initial build (missing `GET` handler; `activeGrant`/`grant` and `effectivePlan`/`plan` response-key mismatch; snake_case vs camelCase grant fields) were fixed before ship and `npx tsc --noEmit` passes clean. **Breaking changes:** None. **Chain:** `dev-database` -> `dev-backend` + `dev-frontend` -> `security-auth-guardian` + `quality-code-reviewer` -> docs. **Web-only — no iOS work needed:** iOS reads the same `profiles.plan`, so a granted tier is inherited automatically (see the `IOS_PARITY.md` 2026-06-14 row).

- fix(settings): **Make every settings control truthful (web + iOS)** (web + iOS; committed not pushed; zero AI cost). A sweep that deleted placebo controls and wired the ones that stayed to real enforcement, so no toggle lies about what it does. **WEB ENFORCEMENT — the privacy toggles now actually do something server-side:** (1) **Leaderboard exclusion enforced.** "Appear on leaderboards" off now removes the user from every public ladder. `lib/db.ts` `getLeaderboard` / `getLadderLeaderboard` (Quiz Duel / Competitive / Squad) + the weekly Fangs ladder all (a) `.eq("profile_visibility", "public")` in SQL so `friends`/`private` profiles never surface, then (b) post-filter in JS via the new `isLeaderboardOptedOut(prefs)` helper that drops anyone whose `preferences.privacy.show_on_leaderboard` is `false`/`"false"` (over-fetch headroom keeps the page full after the filter). (2) **Duel-from `nobody` returns a 403.** `app/api/arena/challenge/route.ts` POST now reads the target's `preferences.privacy.duel_from` and refuses with 403 "This user isn't accepting duel challenges" BEFORE inserting the `arena_challenge`, so a blocked challenge never reaches the inbox (absent pref defaults to `everyone`, so missing prefs still allow). (3) **Email / weekly-report column fix.** The academia weekly-digest cron (`app/api/cron/academia-digest/route.ts`) now reads the EMAIL channel `preferences.notifications_email.weekly_report` instead of the in-app `notifications.weekly_report` key — the In-app and Email checkboxes are independent channels, and the email defaults ON (`DEFAULT_PREFERENCES.notifications_email` seeds `weekly_report:true`), so it skips only when the email toggle is explicitly `false`. (4) **Notification delivery gated per-key AND on quiet hours.** `notifyUser` in `lib/db.ts` gates every insert through `shouldNotifyUser(userId, prefKey)` (hard per-key mute) then `isInQuietHours(userId)` (soft, time-boxed; honors `quiet_hours_enabled` + `quiet_hours_start`/`end`, fail-open so a bad blob can't permanently mute); the duel-challenge ping routes through it on `duel_challenges`. **REMOVED DEAD TOGGLES:** the privacy page (`app/settings/privacy/page.tsx`) dropped the "show online status" toggle (no presence system reads it) and the "show Fang balance" toggle (nothing gated on it), and collapsed the duel-challenge + friend-request controls from a 3-option to **Everyone / Nobody** to match the `everyone|nobody`-only contract `sanitizePrivacy` actually persists (the old `friends` value was silently dropped server-side). **NEW APPEARANCE SECTION + FIXED THEME CONTROL:** new `app/settings/appearance/page.tsx` is the discoverable home for Personalization — a Theme card (Dark / Light) and a Font size card, plus a pointer to `/profile` for cosmetics + identity. The Theme control is now truthful: it rides the EXACT same pipeline the profile page's PersonalizationSection uses (write `localStorage`, mutate `<html>` `dataset.theme` + toggle the `light` class, dispatch `themechange`, persist via `updatePreferences`), so Dark/Light actually applies app-wide and survives reload instead of being a no-op. Added to the settings nav rail (`app/settings/layout.tsx`) as the 2nd section with a Palette icon. **LIMELIGHT NAV REDESIGN:** the settings nav rail's active-state limelight was redesigned — a framer-motion shared `layoutId` pill (`settingsNavLimelight` desktop / `settingsNavLimelightPill` mobile) that animates between routes with a per-row `--limelight` accent (electric blue on normal sections, red ONLY on Danger Zone so the red glow can't bleed onto a non-danger section), reduced-motion collapses the spring to 0. **Migration required:** No (reuses the `060`/JSONB preference columns from the settings overhaul). **Breaking changes:** None. **Chain:** `dev-backend` + `dev-frontend` (web) + `ios-dev-data` (iOS) -> `quality-code-reviewer` + `security-auth-guardian` + `ios-code-reviewer` -> docs. iOS counterpart logged in the same-day `IOS_PARITY.md` row + `lionade-ios/docs/CHANGELOG.md`.

- feat(party): **New Party game "Trivia" (Lightning Round) + Bluff stall/dedup fixes + secret-column hardening** (commit `70d7016`; web-only, committed not pushed). **(1) Trivia (Lightning Round) — Kahoot-style MCQ race ADDED to the Party suite** (code id `trivia`, display name "Lightning Round"; Bluff is untouched and stays fully present, this is an addition not a replacement). Flow: lobby pick, then a 5s countdown, then a ~12s answer phase where everyone taps one of 4 options as a single immutable pick, then a ~6s reveal (the correct option turns green, points = base 500 + speed bonus + streak bonus, the leaderboard re-sorts), then the next round, then a Game Over podium after N rounds (default 10). **Server-authoritative phase timers:** `trivia_rounds.answer_ends_at` / `reveal_ends_at` drive the deadlines; phase advance is a compare-and-swap with a GET-route lazy-advance plus an any-member fallback, so a backgrounded host can't freeze the room, and an "everyone answered early" check shortens the answer deadline. Questions reuse the existing free OpenTriviaDB feed + curated fallback bank, so **ZERO new API cost.** New files: `components/party/TriviaView.tsx`, `components/party/AvatarCheckRow.tsx` (extracted from `BluffView` for shared submit-checkmark rows), `lib/party/trivia-questions.ts`, `lib/party/trivia-advance.ts`, `app/api/party/trivia/rounds/route.ts` + `[id]/{route,answer,complete}.ts`. Lionade Party live-playtest fix batch (Sam playtested with real players; 6 commits, all web-only, no migration, committed not pushed).

- fix(party): **Invites worked for nobody, including the host** (commit `e7349f8`). Every invite returned "Join the room before inviting friends." Root cause: the in-room membership checks did `.select("id")` on `party_room_players`, which has a composite PK `(room_id, user_id)` and **no `id` column**, so PostgREST errored, the error was silently discarded as `data: null`, and the in-room check failed for everyone. Fix: select a real column + `limit(1)` + capture/log the error instead of swallowing it; the join route's fresh-join is now an upsert on `(room_id, user_id)`; the page auto-join is idempotent via a ref. Delivery: after the notifications insert the server also broadcasts on `notifs-<friendId>`, the Navbar's channel listens for that broadcast and re-emits to the invite bus (deduped by notification id). `PartyInviteToast` restyled to a right-side slide-in with a 5s auto-dismiss (was top-center, 30s).
- fix(party): **Bluff Trivia "didn't work" — 8 breaks fixed** (commit `5c33917`). The vote phase randomly skipped (the advance-lock released early and a stale-phase re-POST advanced vote->reveal with zero votes); scores were double-applied; a non-host could freeze on a missed ROUND_STARTED; per-round channel churn caused deafness plus throwaway send-channels; nobody advanced when the host tab was backgrounded; a second forfeiter 409'd; a round-create race left an infinite spinner. Fixes: compare-and-swap phase transitions (`UPDATE ... WHERE phase = from`) where only the CAS winner scores and reveal is terminal; a `from_phase` stale-intent guard; `adoptRound` + a seen-set for continuous adoption; a single per-room subscription; any-member advance after the deadline + grace; create idempotency + an 8s loading-rescue retry button.
- fix(party): **Sketchy guess overlay was blocking the canvas + guess display rebuilt** (commit `4430101`). The "overlay blocking the canvas" was the word-blanks mask pill absolutely positioned over the canvas; moved into normal flow. Guesses are now panel-only: a correct guess renders a green "[name] got it! ✓" with the word never shown to non-guessers, a wrong guess renders as small muted gray. Canvas widened to fill viewport height (`max-w-7xl`, dvh-sized at the 1000x600 logical space); the guesses panel narrowed to 260px.
- fix(party): **Sketchy 16-color paper palette** (commit `310247c`). New 16-color palette as a 4x4 grid of 28px swatches with a cream selected ring. The canvas surface was flipped from near-black to paper (`#EEF4FF`) because the mandated palette's dark inks (black/navy/dark gray) were invisible on the old dark canvas.
- fix(party): **Sketchy round 1 was dead + a word-leak bug** (commit `1f54d22`). Round 1 was dead: the lobby START raced clients' channel subscribe (and the host's own subscribe), so ROUND_STARTED for round 1 was sent to a channel nobody had joined, and if the missed client was the drawer no word was picked. Fixed with the BluffView adoption pattern: a shared `adoptRound` + seen-set fed by broadcast + a 3s snapshot poll (the snapshot now carries public round facts including a `word_picked` boolean, never the word), the drawer fetches `/words` on every adoption path, and host auto-start is gated on the channel reaching SUBSCRIBED with a 4s fallback. Word leak: a near-miss "close" guess matched ALL positions of the secret (`matchLetterPositions` returns every positional match) and lit the whole word green mid-round; fixed server-authoritatively with a hidden floor (1/3 of letter cells, min 1) that guesses can never reveal, so the round-end reveal stays the first time non-drawers see the word.
- fix(party): **Systemic connectivity fix — channel ownership** (commit `dfd71e2`). supabase-js dedupes channels BY TOPIC and removes by topic with an async leave, so `page.tsx` + `RoomLobby` shared one `party-room-{code}` instance and RoomLobby's unmount at game start killed the page's channel (GAME_ENDED/PLAYER_JOINED went poll-only in-game); teardown+recreate on `roomId` raced the async leave and could permanently kill the channel; throwaway-channel sends could dedupe onto and kill live channels. Fixes: the page is the sole owner, created once; the players `postgres_changes` listener moved to a dedicated `party-room-{code}-players` topic; RoomLobby attaches handlers to the page-owned channel via a prop; `PokerFaceView` ported to single-subscription + `adoptRound` (its six throwaway sends now ride the subscribed channel); all sends are get-or-create-never-remove; the straggler nudge uses `subscribeResilient`; tab-close leave now broadcasts PLAYER_LEFT server-side; a `visibilitychange` refresh was added. Every game transition is now a fast-path broadcast on a resilient channel with the 3s poll as reconciler.

**Migration required:** No (this batch). **Breaking changes:** None. Web-only; wire-contract notes for the eventual iOS port logged in the `IOS_PARITY.md` 2026-06-11 entry.

> **Operator note — verify prod migrations.** Per the supabase migration list, several local-only migrations appear unapplied to prod, including `supabase/migrations/20260605230000_bluff_answers_truth_fake_coexist.sql` and the `20260607_party_v2.sql` / `20260610_party_word_difficulty.sql` / `20260610_sketch_bank_source.sql` / `20260610_class_assignments.sql` party + academia migrations. Run `db push` / verify before relying on those columns and tables in prod.

## 2026-06-10

- feat(competitive): **2v2 duo create/join + networked round start** (commit `73e2de0`). Web-only, zero AI. **(1) 2v2 duo create/join UI:** the arena hub 2v2 toggle (previously a "coming" placeholder) now offers Create duo (mints a 4-digit code to share), Join duo (enter a teammate's code), or Solo (auto-pair). Two friends queueing 2v2 with the same `partyCode` land on the same team. Backend matchmaking already grouped by `party_code`; this commit supplies the missing UI. The 1v1 flow and the stale-closure 45s timeout are untouched. Reviewer APPROVED. **(2) Networked round start:** each client used to run its own 3-2-1-GO countdown on mount, so clock skew + load time handed one player a head start. `competitive_matches` now carries a server-set `starts_at` (= `created_at` + 4.5s lead, migration `059`), the Countdown anchors to it, and each mode screen anchors round 1's clock to `starts_at` so both clients begin in lockstep. A late loader clamps to now (disadvantages only the late player, no edge), and the flow falls back to the local sequence when `starts_at` is null. Reviewer APPROVED; per-round full sync deferred. **Deferred (not shipped):** a server-authoritative Sabotage-attack version was built and then code-review BLOCKED and reverted — it measured answer speed against `sabotage_rounds.started_at` (seed-time, not real per-round start, so it wrongly rejected legit attacks on rounds 2-8); its read-check-insert wasn't atomic (double-spend / cooldown-bypass race, no serializing constraint on `sabotage_attacks`); and the attack EFFECT is an unauthenticated client broadcast, so the server ledger gate didn't actually close the grief vector. A proper fix needs a deterministic authoritative per-round start origin shared client+server, an atomic insert (a unique cooldown-bucket constraint like the `/answer` route), and server-validated effect delivery. Logged as tech debt for a next pass, NOT shipped. **Migration required:** Yes, `059` (`competitive_matches` gains a `starts_at` column) — **applied to prod.** **Breaking changes:** None. Web-only; iOS parity gap folded into the `IOS_PARITY.md` 2026-06-10 competitive entry.
- feat(competitive): **ELO-integrity gate + connectivity + forfeit/void** (commit `ff0d373`). New principle enforced everywhere: **you only earn ELO if you actually played against someone.** New `lib/competitive/settle.ts` `settleClaimedMatch` is the single shared settle funnel for `/complete`, `/forfeit`, and the reaper. ELO + Fangs settle ONLY when BOTH teams recorded `>=1 competitive_response`; a no-show / instant disconnect VOIDS the match (status `voided`) with NO `profiles` ELO/Fang write at all (`elo_after = elo_before`, zero Fang delta, no penalty to the player who showed). A mid-match quit where both played settles normally. New `POST /api/competitive/match/[id]/forfeit` (participant-only) voids with no penalty if the opponent never engaged, else forces the caller's loss and settles, using the same atomic `active`->`completing` claim as `/complete` so it can't double-fire. New `/api/cron/reap-stale-competitive` (CRON_SECRET bearer auth) resolves hung/AFK matches through the same gate so a match can't hang forever; scheduled in `vercel.json` every 3 min — **the reaper needs `CRON_SECRET` set on Vercel to run.** Connectivity: `use-match-channel` now reconnects via `subscribeResilient` + adds Supabase Presence, exposing `connection` / `opponentPresent` / `opponentLastSeen` (gameplay protocol + the 4 mode screens unchanged). UI: a Reconnecting banner, an opponent-disconnected panel (End Match -> `/complete` which voids if the opponent never played, or Keep Waiting), an explicit Forfeit (-> `/forfeit`), and VOIDED ("no Elo or Fangs changed") + FORFEITED result states in `ResultCard`/`useSettle`. Reviewer APPROVED, no blockers: the gate is unbypassable (all 3 settle paths funnel through the one function; void is a true `profiles` no-op). Known debt (deferred, non-blocking): a process crash in the sub-second settle window can leave a match stuck in `completing`; recovering it race-free needs an `entered_completing_at` timestamp. **Migration required:** Yes, `058` (`competitive_matches` gains `voided` + `forfeited` statuses + a `forfeited_by` column) — **applied to prod.** **Breaking changes:** None. Web-only; iOS parity gap logged in the `IOS_PARITY.md` 2026-06-10 competitive entry.

- feat(academia): **ICS calendar import** (commit `e544148`). New `POST /api/academia/import-ics` runs in two modes: `{ url }` previews and `{ classId, events }` commits the selected events as assignments. A hand-rolled RFC 5545 parser (no dependency) extracts VEVENT `SUMMARY` + `DTSTART` (all date/datetime forms), so a Canvas / Google / Outlook / Apple calendar feed becomes class assignments. Heavy SSRF defense: http(s) only, DNS-resolve then block private / loopback / link-local / CGNAT / cloud-metadata ranges for every resolved address (including IPv4-mapped-IPv6), `redirect: manual` with per-hop re-validation, a pinned-lookup that closes the DNS-rebinding TOCTOU, an 8s timeout, a 2MB cap, a `BEGIN:VCALENDAR` sniff, and generic error messages. The Academia hub gets an "Import calendar" BottomSheet: paste a URL, preview the parsed events with per-event select + a class picker, then import. Rate limited 10/min. Zero API cost. **Migration required:** No. **Breaking changes:** None. Web-only; iOS parity gap logged in the `IOS_PARITY.md` 2026-06-10 Academia entry.

Opt-in is `profiles.preferences.notifications.weekly_report != false`; the run skips opted-out and empty-digest users, escapes all user-supplied strings, and caps at 500 users per run ordered by `created_at`. Scheduled in `vercel.json` for Monday 13:00 UTC. A live send only fires on Vercel with both `CRON_SECRET` and `RESEND` configured. Zero API cost. **Migration required:** No. **Breaking changes:** None. Web-only (server-side, platform-agnostic); see the `IOS_PARITY.md` 2026-06-10 Academia entry.

A duel that resolves with 0 questions now renders an error card instead of a blank null page. **(2) Error states (DiscoverTab house pattern: skeleton, then ErrorState with retry, then true empty state):** class detail 404/not-found card, academia onboarding-gate error card (was an infinite spinner), classes list, vocab banks, GradeTracker, FlashcardStudy, wallet ledger, PastLobbiesPanel, mastery targets. ## 2026-06-06

- fix(ui): unhide Mastery quota pill — move out of LaunchDock collision (commit `ba8e237`). The quota pill was floating bottom-right on `/learn/mastery/[examId]` and colliding with the global LaunchDock "+" button, making it unreadable. Moved into the page header next to the elapsed-time chip.
- fix(vocab): send valid `definition_source` — client omitted required field (commit `d09047e`). `AddWordForm.handleSave` shipped without `definition_source`, so the API 400'd with the raw validator string "must be wikipedia, ai, or manual" reaching the user. Client now passes the source from state with a `"manual"` fallback. Same pass picked up adjacent missing `source_lang` / `target_lang` on the language path and a wrong `coinsAwarded` toast read.
- fix(party): unstick Sketchy round-end — stale host pointer deadlock (commit `69d3b85`). When the host disconnected, `room.host_user_id` stayed pointed at them and every remaining player saw only "Waiting for host". Fix: client-side effective-host derivation (longest-connected active player, deterministic via sorted player list), a visible 12s auto-advance countdown on the reveal phase, and a 6s fallback unlock so non-effective-host clients also get a START NEXT ROUND button.
- fix(party): Bluff Trivia vote save — host self-collision on truth row (commit `873354b`). `bluff_answers` had `UNIQUE (round_id, user_id)`; the round-create endpoint stored the truth row with `user_id=host`, so when the host submitted their own fake the INSERT collided and 500'd, and the bleed-through error read "Couldn't save answer" during the vote phase. Migration relaxes the constraint to `UNIQUE (round_id, user_id, is_truth)`. Route self-heals existing rounds. Client clears stale error on phase change.
- fix(copy): Pro perks — fix Popups gone typo + strip em-dash (commit `4968d64`). Stripped 3 em-dashes from pricing tier-card perks in `app/pricing/page.tsx`. "Popups zone" was a screenshot misread, source already correct.

## 2026-06-05

- fix(ux): kill stale Resume banner — dashboard re-pinning daily_drill. Root cause: `app/api/daily-drill/route.ts` GET handler unconditionally called `setActiveSession(userId, "daily_drill", today, "player")` on every read. `DailyDrillWidget` SWRs that endpoint on every dashboard mount, focus, and 30s revalidation, so the `active_session` pointer + `presence_heartbeats` row got re-pinned forever, defeating both prior fixes (commit `8a90ed7` client staleness window, commit `13240e2` server AFK reaper) because the timestamps were always fresh. Fix: removed the pin from `/api/daily-drill` GET (a read endpoint) and moved it into `app/api/daily-drill/state` GET, which is only called by `DrillModal` on open (actual user intent to play). Lesson logged in [[Tech-Debt]]: read endpoints must never write presence. Web-only — see `IOS_PARITY.md` for the no-row entry.
- fix(games): Games Shakedown P0 sweep — 3 of 4 P0 tester-blockers from `docs/GAMES_SHAKEDOWN_2026-06-05.md` shipped (Timeline drag-on-touch deferred — needs ~2h with a `<DraggableRow>` component). **(1) Pardy Skip closes modal without marking tile attempted** — `app/games/pardy/page.tsx` Skip button used to call `onClose` directly, leaving the tile live; the game-over trigger requires `totalAttempted >= 25`, so a single Skip made FINAL TALLY unreachable. New `skipTile` callback marks the tile `{ attempted: true, correct: false, awarded: 0 }` (matches the wrong-answer state mutation, no Fang grant, no affirmation), threads through `<PardyModal>` via a new `onSkip` prop, and clears the close timer alongside. Also surfaces a `pdfError` toast ("No N-letter words found in this PDF") when `startRoardle` is called with an empty Library source instead of silently no-op'ing. **(3) Flashcards empty Library deck → NaN divide-by-zero** — `app/games/page.tsx` Flashcards in Library mode with an empty `pdfContent.vocabulary` array landed in game state with `fcCards.length === 0`, immediately hit `(fcKnew + n) / 0 = NaN` in `fcAnswer`, and shipped `awardFangs(NaN)` to `/api/games/reward` (which stores NaN to the DB). `startFlashcards` now refuses empty decks with a `pdfError` toast ("No vocab found in this PDF. Try a different document."). Belt-and-suspenders: `fcAnswer`'s pct calc guards `fcCards.length > 0`, and the game-over render guards the percent display the same way. **Cross-game autoCorrect sweep** — `autoCorrect="off" autoCapitalize="off" autoComplete="off" spellCheck={false}` added to every game text input the shakedown report flagged (single highest-ROI sweep — iPhone auto-cap silently invalidates guesses across half the suite, exact mechanism of today's Roardle-class bug): Bluff fake-answer input (`components/party/BluffView.tsx`), Pardy answer textarea (`app/games/pardy/page.tsx`), Resume Coach Socratic textarea (`components/Coach/SocraticBubble.tsx`), Mastery Socratic textarea (`components/Mastery/MasteryActionArea.tsx`), Mastery landing parse + narrow-down textareas (`app/learn/mastery/page.tsx`). **Sketchy guess input deliberately deferred** — Bucket C agent is editing `components/party/SketchView.tsx` for the Rematch CTA this session; the one-line autoCorrect attrs will be applied as a follow-up post-Bucket-C land. - fix(web): Sketchy realtime — broadcasts now use a single subscribed channel ref, eliminating the silent drop on fresh tabs / slow networks (drawer was missing round-won events). Root cause: every send site (`SketchView.tsx` ROUND_STARTED / WORD_SELECTED / LETTER_REVEAL / GUESS / ROUND_ENDED; `SketchCanvas.tsx` STROKE / CLEAR_CANVAS / undo) created a fresh `supabase.channel(...)` handle and called `.send()` on it without awaiting `.subscribe()`. Supabase silently no-ops sends on an unsubscribed channel handle, so the first GUESS-correct on a slow connection vanished and the drawer's UI stayed mid-round with `iGotIt=true` on the guesser only. Fix: lifted a `channelRef` + `subscribedRef` per component, populated from the existing listener `useEffect` (status callback flips `subscribedRef` on SUBSCRIBED/CLOSED/CHANNEL_ERROR/TIMED_OUT). New `sendBroadcast(event, payload)` helper awaits `.send()`, checks the return status, and retries once after 150ms before logging. SketchCanvas mid-stroke 30Hz ticks skip the retry (per-frame loss is imperceptible; the final stroke broadcast in onPointerUp is authoritative). Channel name unchanged. Server-side broadcast path deferred to a separate spec. Files: `components/party/SketchView.tsx`, `components/party/SketchCanvas.tsx`. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean (only pre-existing `app/games/page.tsx:760` error remains). Chain: `dev-realtime-web` (diagnosis + fix) → self-pass `quality-code-reviewer` mental checklist → `quality-docs-writer` (this entry + IOS_PARITY row + vault Daily/2026-05-31.md).

## 2026-05-29

- feat(web): **Party lobby flavor — rotating "hurry up bro" nudge + host "setting things up" thinking dots (web-only, iOS paused).** Two small fun additions to the Party lobby Sam asked for after the 2-player playtest. (1) **Rotating nudge button.** Non-hosts get a "👉 NUDGE THE HOST" button in the lobby, but only ONE non-host has it at a time. Active nudger derived deterministically from wall-clock + the active non-host list (`Math.floor(Date.now() / 45_000) % nonHosts.length`) so every client picks the same person without a server arbiter; rotates every 45s. Tapping picks a random phrase from a 20-item list (`"hurry up bro" / "tick tock" / "did your wifi die?" / "respectfully, start the game" / "we believe in you king"` etc., family-safe Gen-Z, no em-dashes, never mean) and broadcasts it on a NEW `nudgeChannel(code)` separate from the room-state channel so its handlers don't tangle with the room lifecycle. Everyone in the room sees a fixed-top toast with the sender's name + phrase ("Brother: 'hurry up bro'") that springs in and self-prunes after 3.5s, max 4 stacked. Supabase broadcast doesn't echo to sender, so the sender gets a local-echo toast immediately. After a tap the button enters a "NUDGE SENT · NEXT TURN IN A SEC" cooldown until the next 45s window. No DB, no auth changes, no secret surface — pure ephemeral chrome. (2) **Host "setting things up" indicator.** Below the room code on non-host screens, a quiet "Host is setting things up" line with three pulsing dots (reuses the existing `pa-ink-dot` keyframe at 200ms staggered delay, reduced-motion guarded). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No em-dashes in copy.
