- fix(web): **Party 2-player playtest triage — Sketchy drawer-non-host blank picker + Vercel candidates cache + Bluff/Poker Face min-2 (web-only, iOS paused).** Sam playtested with 2 players on prod after the earlier Poker Face + Sketchy redesign pushes and hit three real bugs. (1) **Sketchy "Your turn! but no cards"** — root cause: the fair-random drawer change earlier today (`235e692`+) meant the drawer can be a non-host, but `SketchView.tsx`'s `ROUND_STARTED` broadcast handler that informs the drawer-non-host of the round only set `phase='select-word'` + ninny="Your turn!" without ever calling `apiGet('/api/party/sketch/rounds/[id]/words')` — that fetch was host-only inside `startRound`. So the drawer-non-host landed on the picker block (`phase==='select-word' && candidates`) with `candidates=null`, which renders nothing → blank screen with the ninny still there, and nothing to press. Fix: the broadcast handler now fetches `/words` when `isMe=true` (same drawer-only auth path the host uses), falling back to drawing phase + a clear ninny line if the fetch fails. (2) **Sketchy candidates cache unreliable on Vercel** — the candidate set was held in a per-process in-memory cache (`lib/party/sketch-candidates.ts`), so the `POST /rounds` that deals the round and the `GET /words` that fetches the candidates can land on DIFFERENT lambda instances, with the GET reading an empty cache and returning 410. Fix: persisted `candidate_words` JSONB on `sketch_rounds` via **migration 058** (`20260529010000_sketch_candidate_words.sql`, applied to remote); deal route writes the column; `/words` reads from the row (drawer-only via 403); `/select-word` validates against the row. The column inherits the existing `sketch_rounds` RLS (migration 055 hardening) — secret-safe by construction. The in-memory cache is kept as a warm-path fallback for any in-flight pre-058 round. (3) **Bluff + Poker Face refused 2-player rooms** — Sam tested with 2 (him + brother on a call) but both games required 3+. Lowered the min to 2 in `app/api/party/rooms/[code]/start/route.ts`, `RoomLobby.tsx` GAME_META (`minPlayers: 2`), and the pokerface deal route. Degenerate at 2 (Poker Face: presenter rotates between two, the only caller IS the interrogator — playable for testing) but unblocks the duo flow. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean; migration applied to remote (`npx supabase db push`); no em-dashes in copy. **iOS: paused per CEO web-only Party scope.** Chain: bug triage from the screenshot → `dev-frontend` (broadcast-handler fetch) + `dev-backend` (DB column + route reads) + `dev-database` (migration 058) + `dev-frontend` (lobby min) → `quality-code-reviewer` → `quality-docs-writer` (this entry + IOS_PARITY + vault).
- feat(web): **Poker Face — the Interrogation + "same room OR call" reframe + how-to-play rules (web-only, iOS paused; committed locally, push pending Sam playtest).** Follow-up to the Poker Face deep pass, all greenlit by Sam. (1) **Call reframe.** Sam's insight: the spoken/face mode isn't physical-proximity-only, a video/voice call (e.g. him + his brother) works identically. The real axis is "can you see/hear each other live," not same-room. Relabeled the lobby toggle **SAME ROOM OR CALL** (spoken/live) vs **TEXT ONLY** (typed), with matching banner + footnote copy in `RoomLobby.tsx` + `PokerFaceView.tsx`. Stored value `pf_mode` stays `inperson`/`remote`; only the labels/copy changed. (2) **The Interrogation** (the standout depth mechanic from the design pass). In live mode, after the presenter commits, the round enters a new `interrogate` phase: one rotating caller (the active player seated right after the presenter, by join order) gets to grill the presenter with ONE question out loud before calls open. The tell isn't the claim, it's how they handle the follow-up. NO migration: the `phase` column is unconstrained text, and the interrogator is derived deterministically server-side (identical logic in the GET route + the new `open-vote` route, verified consistent by `quality-code-reviewer`). New `POST /api/party/pokerface/rounds/[id]/open-vote` advances `interrogate -> vote` (host OR interrogator authorized; race-guarded; resets `presented_at` so the vote window starts fresh). A 25s timer auto-advances as a backstop, fired by EITHER the host's OR the interrogator's client so a host-drop can't stall the grill. Text-only mode skips the Interrogation (present -> vote directly), since the grill is about reading a live reaction. Secret-safe (reviewer: no Critical): the `interrogate` phase ships nothing secret to callers (is_lie/card_fact stay presenter-gated; RLS still blocks direct client reads since `interrogate != reveal`). (3) **How-to-play rules.** A collapsible HOW TO PLAY block in the Poker Face lobby section (6 numbered rules) so newcomers can learn the game, per Sam's "display rules" ask. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean; `/games/party/[code]` 200, `open-vote`/present 401 unauthed (compiled). No em-dashes in copy. **iOS: paused per CEO web-only Party scope.** Chain: `admin` (design pass) → `dev-backend` (interrogate phase + open-vote route + interrogator derivation) → `dev-frontend` (interrogate UI + timer + reframe + rules) → `design-copywriter` (call reframe + rules + grill copy) → `quality-code-reviewer` (no leak; fixed the host-drop stall MEDIUM + a stale phase cast) → `quality-docs-writer` (this entry + IOS_PARITY + vault).
- feat(web): **Poker Face deep pass — hybrid in-person/remote, win condition + awards, reveal theater, scoring risk (web-only, iOS paused; committed locally, push pending Sam playtest).** A full design + build pass on the Party bluff game after a deep agent design pass (admin → product-strategist + design-ui-ux + design-motion-web + design-copywriter + data-analytics). The diagnosis: the game was branded "the face is the tell" but the lie was TYPED and shown as text, so it played like a slower Bluff Trivia. Fixes, all on the existing 3-phase server-authoritative loop, NO migration (settings live in `party_rooms.settings` JSONB): (1) **Hybrid mode (the fork fix).** The host picks **Same Room** (default) vs **Remote** in the lobby (`components/party/RoomLobby.tsx`, stored `settings.pf_mode`). In-person: the presenter privately picks truth/lie with NO text box (a compose beat + "OPEN THE TABLE"), the claim is SPOKEN aloud, `claim_text` is stored null for both truth and lie (`present/route.ts` reads `pf_mode`), and callers see no text, just "they made their claim out loud, did you buy it?" + BELIEVE/DOUBT. Remote keeps the typed-claim flow. In-person ships strictly LESS data, so the secret-leak posture (migration `20260528020000` RLS + presenter-gated GET) is preserved or tighter (verified by `quality-code-reviewer`: no Critical leaks). (2) **Win condition + end-game awards.** Games now END after `pf_rotations` full rotations (host picks 1/2/3, default 2; `round_num >= rotations * player_count`). Player count is FROZEN at game start (`settings.pf_player_count`) so a mid-game leaver can't shrink the length. The reveal then shows a GAME OVER awards screen: **Bluff Master** (most callers fooled) + **Human Lie Detector** (most correct reads), tallied client-side across the game (best-effort/local — cosmetic, the server-authoritative scoreboard decides the real winner). (3) **Scoring risk.** Added `POKERFACE_CAUGHT_PENALTY = 200`: a lie the WHOLE room doubts (zero fooled) docks the presenter 200, so lying isn't free. A single shared `pokerFaceRoundPoints()` helper (`lib/party/scoring.ts`) now powers BOTH the authoritative complete-route banking AND the reveal-GET preview, so displayed == banked exactly; the score floor was removed so a blown bluff can go negative (preview/score parity, fitting badge of shame). (4) **Reveal theater.** Verdict slams in (`pa-stamp`), the real fact always surfaces (`pa-factoid-up`, educational payoff every round, truth or lie), call-out rows deal in staggered (`pa-deal-in`) with correct reads flashing green (`pa-correct-flash`); GPU-only, reduced-motion guarded. (5) **8 new fact cards** (`lib/party/pokerface-cards.ts`, verifiable + family-safe, word-unique) + mode-aware Ninny host lines + a "ROUND X OF N" header + a mode-aware banner. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean; `/games/party/[code]` 200, pokerface API routes 401 unauthed (compiled). No em-dashes in copy. Known V1 limitations (logged, defensible for a party game): awards tally is client-local (late joiners undercount); win-condition is client-derived (no server end-of-game row). **iOS: paused per CEO web-only Party scope.** Chain: `admin` (deep design orchestration) → `dev-backend` (mode-aware present + start settings merge + shared scoring helper + penalty) → `dev-frontend` (hybrid present/vote screens + end-game awards + reveal theater) → `design-motion-web` (`pa-*` reveal choreography) → `design-copywriter` (cards + host lines) → `quality-code-reviewer` (no leak; fixed the preview/banked HIGH + win-condition drift MEDIUM) → `quality-docs-writer` (this entry + IOS_PARITY + vault Daily/2026-05-29).
- feat(web): **Sketchy Subjects — word-picker redesign + fair-random first drawer (web-only, iOS paused).** Two fixes from Sam's playtest: the word-selection screen "was too blank," and the room creator was always forced to draw first. (1) **Word-picker redesign** (`components/party/SketchView.tsx`, `select-word` phase): color-coded **difficulty badges** (easy green / medium amber / hard rose) replace the plain text; a per-word **"i" info popover** showing the word's MEANING + an IN A SENTENCE example (fetched client-side from the free Dictionary API — drawer-only screen, so the candidate words are already on this client and nothing leaks to guessers) plus the DID YOU KNOW factoid as a guaranteed base that always renders even when the dictionary has no entry; a **10-second auto-pick countdown ring** (purple → red under 3s) that picks a random candidate if the drawer stalls, so a round can never hang on word selection; and a **"WAITING TO GUESS" strip** listing the other players with a "charging" green dot (`pa-charge` keyframe, reduced-motion guarded) so the screen feels alive instead of empty. The drawer now needs the factoid, so `GET /api/party/sketch/rounds/[id]/words` (already 403 for non-drawers) includes it in the candidate payload — no guesser exposure. (2) **Fair-but-random first drawer** (`app/api/party/sketch/rounds/route.ts`): replaced the deterministic `(round_num - 1) % players` pick (which always made the first-joined player — the host/creator — draw round 1) with a least-drawn-random pick: count each active player's prior `drawer_user_id` rounds, take the minimum, and pick randomly among players at that minimum. Round 1 (everyone at 0) is fully random; every rotation still has each player draw exactly once before anyone repeats (fairness preserved, order varied). `Math.random` is fine here (drawer choice is not security-sensitive, unlike room codes). A double-pick guard (`pickedRef`) stops the manual tap and the auto-pick from both firing; the server already rejects a second `select-word` with 409 as a backstop. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean; `/games/party` + `/games/party/[code]` 200 on the dev server. No em-dashes in user-facing copy. Sam's optional "chat on the picker" was deferred (the waiting strip + countdown already fill the space; a real chat needs its own channel). **iOS: paused per CEO web-only scope.** Chain: `admin` → `dev-frontend` (picker UI + countdown + info popover + waiting strip) → `dev-backend` (random drawer + words-route factoid) → `design-motion-web` (`pa-charge` + countdown ring) → `security-auth-guardian` (factoid stays on the drawer-only route; secret word still server-side) → `quality-code-reviewer` (tsc clean) → `quality-docs-writer` (this entry + IOS_PARITY row + vault Daily/2026-05-29).
- feat(web): **Sketchy Subjects v2 — color picker, shared guesses panel, Wordle letter-reveal, Fang reward faucet, expanded words (web-only, iOS paused).** Five upgrades from Sam's playtest. (1) **Color picker** in `SketchToolbar` — keeps 8 quick swatches, adds an expandable 48-swatch spectrum grid + native `<input type="color">` for any custom color; flows through the existing single color source, stroke-sync untouched. (2) **Shared guesses panel** — the guesser-only chat is now a room-wide panel visible to everyone incl. the drawer. (3) **Wordle-style letter reveal** — guessers see the target as blank boxes (length + punctuation shown); `lib/party/letter-reveal.ts` runs server-side in `/guess` and returns ONLY matched green positions (the secret word NEVER reaches guesser clients, preserving the migration-055 RLS posture); correct-position letters light green on both the panel guess and the shared blanks; full-correct still wins. Live updates ride a new low-frequency `LETTER_REVEAL` broadcast (separate from the 30Hz stroke flood); late joiners catch up via `GET /reveal`. (4) **Fang reward faucet (NOT a wager)** — `lib/party/sketch-economy.ts` + `sketch-fangs.ts`: per correct guess 3 + order bonus (3/2/1/0), per revealed correct-position letter 1 (cap 8/player/round), per drawing 2/correct guesser (cap 10/round); ~24 Fangs/round, below one quiz session, no PvP transfer, capped both paths so it does not print Fangs. Server-authoritative via service role + idempotent `sketch_fang_awards` ledger + `sketch_revealed_positions` claim table; **migration 057** (`20260529000000_party_sketch_fang_rewards.sql`) applied + registered in remote history. This revises the earlier "Party V1: ZERO Fang stakes" line to a small faucet; the V2 winner-takes-pot idea stays separate + deferred. (5) **Word lists 400 → 752** (~94/subject across 8), reseeded `party_word_lists` (verified 752), zero intra-subject dupes, no em-dashes. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean; `/games/party` 200; Bluff + Poker Face untouched. Chain: `admin` → `data-economist` (reward numbers + inflation check) → `design-copywriter` (word expansion) → `design-ui-ux` → `dev-database` (migration 057) → `dev-backend` (server-side position matching that never ships the secret) → `dev-realtime-web` (guess/reveal broadcasts) → `dev-frontend` → `security-auth-guardian` (secret stays server-side; awards server-authoritative) → `quality-code-reviewer` → `quality-docs-writer`.
- fix(web): **Roardle — physical-keyboard input + standard Wordle duplicate-letter scoring (staged, NOT committed; web-only, iOS paused).** Sam reported two bugs in Roardle (the science-word Wordle game in `/games`, `app/games/page.tsx`): you could only play with the on-screen keyboard, and letter feedback was wrong on words with repeated letters. **BUG 1 — physical keyboard.** There was no `keydown` listener, so the computer keyboard did nothing. Added a scoped `useEffect` (early-returns unless `game === "roardle" && !roardleOver`) that adds a `window` `keydown` handler and tears it down on cleanup / when leaving the game or the round ends. The handler: returns early on any `metaKey/ctrlKey/altKey` combo (does not hijack Cmd/Ctrl/Alt browser/OS shortcuts); returns early when the event target is an `INPUT`/`TEXTAREA`/`SELECT` or `isContentEditable` (does not steal keys from text fields); maps `Enter` → `submitRoardleGuess()` (same path as the on-screen ENTER), `Backspace` → remove last letter, and `^[a-zA-Z]$` → append the uppercased letter up to `wordLength`. Letter/backspace use functional `setRoardleInput` updates so the effect needs no `roardleInput` dep (no stale closure); it depends on `[game, roardleOver, wordLength, submitRoardleGuess]` so submit always sees current state. The on-screen keyboard buttons are untouched, so both input methods work. **BUG 2 — duplicate-letter scoring (the real Wordle rule).** The old `getLetterStatus` used the naive `target.includes(guess[idx])` check, which marks every occurrence of a letter "present" even when the answer has fewer of that letter — e.g. answer WATER (one E) with a guess containing two E's would light both yellow. Replaced with a duplicate-aware `getRowStatuses(guess, target)` two-pass scorer: pass 1 colors greens (correct position) and decrements that letter's remaining count from the answer; pass 2 assigns yellow only while the letter still has remaining count, so surplus duplicate guesses fall through to gray. `getLetterStatus` is kept as a thin delegator to the row scorer (so any single-cell caller is correct too). **All three feedback surfaces now use the correct logic:** the guess grid scores each row once via `getRowStatuses`; `getKeyboardStatus` builds the cumulative per-key state (green > yellow > gray > unused) from `getRowStatuses`; the win/lose/6-guess rules were already standard and unchanged. **Algorithm verified** with a standalone harness — EERIE vs WATER → P/A/P/A/A (one E yellow, surplus E's gray), AAAAA vs WATER → A/C/A/A/A (positional A green, rest gray), WATER vs WATER → all green, ALLOY vs LLAMA and BABES vs ABBEY both score per standard Wordle. **Accessibility:** each scored tile now carries an `aria-label` (`"<letter>, correct position | wrong position | not in word"`) plus a small `aria-hidden` shape glyph (● correct / ◐ present / ○ absent) so feedback is not color-only; the keydown handler attaches to `window` and never moves focus, so it does not trap focus or break tab order. **IP boundary:** mechanics only — Lionade's own science `WORD_BANK` (4/5/6-letter words) and the "Roardle" name are unchanged; NO NYT word list, branding, copy, or assets were introduced. The Lionade-specific 4/5/6 word-length picker, the existing word-bank guess validation ("Not in word list"), and the Fang reward + daily-limit + results screen are all intact. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. `/games` returns 200 on the dev server. No em-dashes in copy. **iOS: paused per CEO web-only scope** — the iOS Games hub has its own fully-ported Roardle (`app/games.tsx`); these are web-side fixes only and will be mirrored when iOS resumes (the duplicate-scoring rule + a RN keyboard equivalent are not relevant to the physical-keyboard fix on touch). Chain: `admin` (orchestration + bug confirmation against code) → `quality-qa-tester` (duplicate-letter, on-screen/physical parity, win/lose, leave-mid-game edge cases) → `dev-frontend` (keydown effect + `getRowStatuses` two-pass scorer + grid/keyboard wire-through) → `design-accessibility` (no focus trap, on-screen keyboard preserved, non-color tile cue) → `quality-code-reviewer` (tsc clean) → `quality-docs-writer` (this entry + FEATURES + IOS_PARITY row + vault Daily/2026-05-29).
- fix(web): **Two Social/friends bugs — slow-to-accept friend requests + search hiding pending-request users (staged, NOT committed; web-only, iOS paused).** Sam reported (1) a sent friend request took ~2 minutes to become acceptable for the recipient, and (2) searching ("look me up") returned nothing for someone who had already sent/received a request. Both confirmed against code, both fixed. **BUG 1 — root cause:** the Social page's pending-requests list (`app/social/page.tsx`) was poll-only — `useSWR("social-friends/<uid>", { refreshInterval: 10000 })` reading a persistent SWR cache that could serve a stale "0 pending". The recipient's NOTIFICATION appeared instantly (the Navbar subscribes a Supabase Realtime INSERT channel on `notifications`), but `friendships` was never wired to realtime, so the Accept option lagged up to the 10s poll behind the notification. **BUG 1 — fix (approach b, no migration):** the EXISTING Navbar notification realtime INSERT channel (`components/Navbar.tsx`, `notifs-<uid>` channel) now reads the inserted notification's `type` and, on `friend_request` or `friend_accepted`, calls `useSWRConfig().mutate('social-friends/<uid>')` so the pending-requests list (recipient) and friends list (sender, on accept) revalidate in ~1s instead of waiting for the poll. This was preferred over publishing `friendships` to `supabase_realtime` (approach a) because it reuses the live notifications channel, needs no migration, leaves `friendships` RLS untouched, AND still covers the sender-sees-acceptance case (the requester gets a `friend_accepted` notification). Safety nets on the `social-friends` hook: poll dropped 10s → 5s and `revalidateOnMount: true` added so a stale persisted cache can no longer mask a request that arrived while the user was away. **BUG 2 — root cause:** `app/api/social/search/route.ts` built an `excludeIds` set from every `accepted` OR `pending` friendship (both directions) and filtered those users out of results entirely, so if A sent B a request, B searching for A got A filtered to nothing. **BUG 2 — fix:** the route no longer hides pending/accepted users. It now returns every match (excluding ONLY self) annotated with a `relationship` field — `"none" | "incoming" | "outgoing" | "friends"` (incoming = they sent ME a request, outgoing = I sent them, friends = accepted) — plus a `friendshipId` for incoming/outgoing rows. The Social search dropdown (`app/social/page.tsx`) renders the right action per result: **none → "Add"** (sends request), **incoming → "Accept"** (accepts the pending request via the same PATCH accept action as the pending list, using the result's `friendshipId`), **outgoing → "Requested"** (disabled), **friends → "Friends"** (disabled, checkmark). So searching for someone who sent you a request now surfaces them with a working Accept button — the key fix for "I searched and nothing came up." The previous single-clickable-row behavior (whole row sent a request) was replaced by per-result action buttons. **Verified (no break):** send/accept/decline/cancel flows still work end-to-end; notifications still fire; friends list still loads; `friendships` reads stay auth-scoped (search relationship lookup filters `or(user_id.eq.me, friend_id.eq.me)`, accept PATCH still requires `friend_id = me AND status = pending`); username search is `ilike %q%` on `profiles.username` (matching confirmed). **Migration: NO** (approach b needed none). **Empirical test (two ephemeral users, real HTTP against the dev server with minted bearer tokens, users cleaned up after):** A → request to B returns success; B's `/api/social/friends` pending list includes A; B searching A's username returns A with `relationship:"incoming"` + a `friendshipId` (Bug 2 confirmed fixed); search still excludes self (no enumeration regression); B accepts via the search result's friendshipId → both A and B appear in each other's friends list; a sequential post-accept search correctly reports `relationship:"friends"`. 8/9 assertions passed on the first concurrent run; the one miss (post-accept search still reading `incoming`) reproduced as a read-after-write replica-lag artifact of firing the search microseconds after the accept commit — an isolated sequential diagnostic confirmed the route returns `friends` correctly, so the logic is sound. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. Routes verified on localhost:3001 (port 3000 in use): `/social` 200, `/api/social/search?q=ab` 401 without auth, `/api/social/friends` 401 without auth. No em-dashes in copy. **iOS: paused per CEO web-only scope** — the iOS Friends/Social screen calls the same backend; the search route's new `relationship` field is additive and backward-compatible, so when iOS resumes it can adopt the Accept-from-search states via-backend with no schema change. Chain: `admin` (orchestration + bug confirmation against code) → `dev-realtime-web` (notification-channel invalidation of `social-friends`, approach b) → `dev-backend` (search `relationship` field + friends-route integrity verify) → `dev-frontend` (search-result Add/Accept/Requested/Friends action states) → `security-auth-guardian` (self-only exclusion preserved, auth-scoped relationship lookups, no user-enumeration regression) → `quality-code-reviewer` (tsc clean) → `quality-docs-writer` (this entry + FEATURES + IOS_PARITY row + vault Daily/2026-05-29).

- feat(web): **Poker Face MOVED from the Competitive arena into Lionade Party as the 3rd party game (staged, NOT committed; web-only).** Sam's call: bluff-reading is a face-to-face social mechanic, not a ranked-vs-strangers skill ladder, so it belongs with Sketchy Subjects + Bluff Trivia. The reframe drops ALL currency: NO ELO, NO Fang wager, NO confidence-wager mechanic (that was a remote crutch — in person the FACE is the tell). Pure points / bragging rights, which also removes the gambling/legal concern entirely. **Added to Party:** N-player (3-8) presenter-rotation — each round the SERVER picks one presenter (rotating through the room by join order so everyone presents before anyone repeats) and deals them a secret fact card; the presenter chooses to present the TRUE fact or invent a LIE and present that claim; everyone else calls BELIEVE or DOUBT; reveal + score; presenter rotates next round. **Scoring matrix (party_room_players.score, server-authoritative):** presenter banks +500 for every caller they fool (believed-a-lie or doubted-a-truth); each caller banks +400 for a correct read (doubt-a-lie or believe-a-truth). **Migration `lib/migrations/056_party_pokerface.sql`** (mirrored to `supabase/migrations/20260528020000_party_pokerface.sql`, dual-location) adds `party_pokerface_rounds` (room_id, round_num, presenter_user_id, card_word, card_fact SECRET, claim_text SECRET, is_lie SECRET, phase present/vote/reveal, started/presented/ended) + `party_pokerface_votes` (round_id, voter_user_id, call believe/doubt, voted_at). **RLS hardened exactly like migration 055:** REVOKE SELECT on both tables from anon + authenticated; `party_pokerface_rounds` gets a presenter-or-revealed SELECT policy (readable directly only at phase='reveal'/ended OR by the presenter); votes are own-row-only; secrets reach callers solely through the service-role GET route. **Migration APPLIED** to remote DB via `npx supabase db push --include-all`; live RLS verified (anon SELECT on `card_fact`/`is_lie`/`claim_text` and on `party_pokerface_votes` both return `42501 permission denied`; service-role reads fine). **Reused the 51 curated fact cards** verbatim — moved into `lib/party/pokerface-cards.ts` (`drawRandomCard(usedWords)` now avoids repeating a card within a room session). **Endpoints under `app/api/party/pokerface/`** (all `requireAuth`-gated, server-authoritative, secrets server-side only): `POST /rounds` (server picks presenter by rotation + deals card secretly, never returns card_fact), `GET /rounds/[id]` (phase-aware sanitized serve path — presenter sees card_fact to choose; callers get only card_word in present, then claim_text in vote; nobody learns is_lie/card_fact before reveal; full reveal + per-round points after), `POST /rounds/[id]/present` (presenter commits truth/lie + claim; if truth the shown claim is FORCED server-side to the true fact so a liar can't masquerade as honest; lie text is player-authored, never generated), `POST /rounds/[id]/call` (presenter can't call own hand; upsert lets a caller change their call during vote), `POST /rounds/[id]/complete` (host-only reveal; atomic vote→reveal phase claim guards against double-score; scores computed ONLY from persisted is_lie + calls). **UI:** new `components/party/PokerFaceView.tsx` (electric-blue accent #00BFFF; present/vote/reveal flow with card-flip + reveal motion; "Best face to face. Gather your crew. The face is the tell." banner; presenter sees their secret fact + Present-the-Truth / Present-the-Lie; callers see the claim + BELIEVE/DOUBT; reveal shows BLUFFED/HONEST + who-was-fooled + scoreboard), wired into the party room shell `app/games/party/[code]/page.tsx`, and added as the 3rd game-select card in `components/party/RoomLobby.tsx`. **"Best played" context badges (Sam's idea — small tasteful glass chips):** party game-select cards now carry Sketchy Subjects = "Either", Bluff Trivia = "Remote OK", Poker Face = "Best in person"; the 4 competitive arena mode cards carry "Remote OK". `current_game` union widened to `'sketch' | 'bluff' | 'pokerface'`; party `/start` route accepts pokerface (min 3 players). **REMOVED from Competitive:** Poker Face dropped from the `/compete/arena` hub mode list + the `[mode]/[matchId]` dispatcher; deleted `components/competitive/pokerface/PokerFaceScreen.tsx`, `app/api/competitive/pokerface/{present,call}/route.ts`, `lib/competitive/pokerface-cards.ts`, and `lib/competitive/pokerface-wager.ts`; pokerface dropped from the `CompetitiveMode` union + `COMPETITIVE_MODES` array (`lib/competitive/types.ts`), from `fang-payout.ts` (removed the pokerface payout row + `pokerFaceParticipation`), from `seed-rounds.ts` (removed the case + `seedPokerFace`), from `channels.ts` (removed the unused HAND event), and from the match GET route + the shared `/complete` route (removed the pokerface-pot winner-derivation + participation branches — competitive winners now always derive from `competitive_responses`). **Competitive arena is now 4 modes: Sabotage, Zoom Reveal, Spectrum, Map Pin** (hub header copy updated "Five" → "Four"). 3 candidate words held in process-local in-memory cache keyed by round id so guessers can't peek), `GET /sketch/rounds/[id]/words` (drawer-only, 403 to others), `POST /sketch/rounds/[id]/select-word`, `POST /sketch/rounds/[id]/strokes` (drawer-only batched persistence with MAX_BATCH=64 and MAX_POINTS_PER_STROKE=2048 caps), `GET /sketch/rounds/[id]/strokes` (late-joiner replay), `POST /sketch/rounds/[id]/guess` (server fuzzy-match; drawer cannot guess; one-correct-per-player gate; persists redacted `[correct]` instead of verbatim guess to avoid word-leak via future DB read), `POST /sketch/rounds/[id]/complete` (drawer-or-host authorized; computes drawer reward; returns reveal payload), `POST /bluff/rounds` (server fetches question + persists truth as a `bluff_answers` row with `is_truth=true` so vote phase can shuffle it in alongside player fakes), `GET /bluff/rounds/[id]` (phase-aware response: write returns has_submitted + submitted_count; vote returns deterministically-seeded-shuffled answers WITHOUT is_truth/author; reveal returns correct_answer + per-answer author + vote_count), `POST /bluff/rounds/[id]/answer` (validates fake != truth via normalize() compare, rejects dupes, upserts), `POST /bluff/rounds/[id]/vote` (cannot vote for own fake, upsert), `POST /bluff/rounds/[id]/complete` (host-only phase advance: write→vote→reveal with vote_ends_at = now + 30s at write→vote transition, applies score deltas on vote→reveal transition). **UI components under `components/party/`**: `RoomCodeShare.tsx`, `PartyScoreboard.tsx`, `NinnyHostBubble.tsx`, `SketchToolbar.tsx` (8 colors + 3 sizes + eraser + undo + clear; Stroke broadcasts use `ch.send({ type: 'broadcast', event: 'stroke', payload })` not table inserts (too slow for 30Hz); server-side stroke persistence is the cold-storage fallback for replay. **Compete page integration**: new "LIONADE PARTY" hero card at `app/compete/page.tsx` between the BLITZ+LEADERBOARD grid and the WEEKLY TOURNAMENT block, glow-purple tilt-card with NEW ribbon, PaintBrush + ChatCircleText subgame pills, links to `/compete/party`. **BackButton update**: `components/BackButton.tsx` adds `/compete/party` → `/compete` parent mapping plus `/^\/compete\/party\/[^/]+$/` dynamic-route regex → `/compete/party`. **Anti-cheat surface**: drawer cannot see chat feed during drawing phase, drawer cannot submit guesses, guess broadcasts redacted to "Got it!" / "Close!" / verbatim-only-on-wrong, server stores `[correct]` literal instead of the verbatim correct guess to prevent word-leak via DB read, no fill bucket / no text tool per locked spec, bluff fake validation rejects normalized matches of the truth answer. **Word list status**: parallel word-curator agent FINISHED `lib/party/word-lists.ts` (400 entries — 50 per subject × 8 subjects — with `WORD_LISTS` + `PartySubject` exports and `WordEntry` shape compatible with the stub). - feat(web): **Arena V2 — Phase 3 ghost-owner offline ELO buffer + Trainer accuracy tune (staged, NOT committed, flag-gated behind `NEXT_PUBLIC_ARENA_V2_ENABLED`).** Web-only per CEO; iOS paused. Closes the two final locked decisions from the 2026-05-26 V2 brainstorm. **(A) Option B ELO conservation.** Every real-ghost match now writes a symmetric +/- ELO update so the rating pool stays conserved at the population level. Live player gets their delta immediately in `/api/arena/v2/complete` (unchanged). Ghost owner is offline so their `−1 × live_delta` is BUFFERED on `profiles.pending_elo_change` (int) + `profiles.pending_elo_summary` (jsonb FIFO-capped at 50 entries) + `profiles.pending_wins/losses/draws`. On next login the V2 lobby renders a `GhostEloCard` ABOVE the subject picker showing "Your ghost ran N duels" + W/L/D row + current to new ELO arrow + Claim button. Trainer-Ninny matches are EXPLICITLY excluded from the conservation system (trainer ghosts inject/absorb ELO from outside the player pool by design; per-user cap of first-3-duels-OR-24h bounds the imbalance). **(B) Trainer accuracy tune-down 75/85/95% to 60/75/90%.** New players win MORE often in their first 3 trainer duels, flipping the trainer cohort from a slight ELO-deflation source to a slight inflation source at launch so cold-start feels competent rather than humbling. **Migration `lib/migrations/050_arena_v2_ghost_elo.sql`** (mirrored to `supabase/migrations/20260526220000_arena_v2_ghost_elo.sql` per the dual-location CLI pattern from 049) adds 5 columns to `profiles` with explanatory `COMMENT ON COLUMN` strings: `pending_elo_change int NOT NULL DEFAULT 0`, `pending_elo_summary jsonb NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]'::jsonb`, `pending_wins int NOT NULL DEFAULT 0`, `pending_losses int NOT NULL DEFAULT 0`, `pending_draws int NOT NULL DEFAULT 0`. **Migration APPLIED** to remote DB via `npx supabase db push --include-all` (Supabase CLI v2.91.2). **Patch `app/api/arena/v2/complete/route.ts`.** Live player ELO computation extracts `liveEloDelta = newLiveElo - liveEloBefore`; ghost-owner delta is `-liveEloDelta`. Selecting `duel_ghosts.owner_user_id` alongside `answers, total_score`. Inside an `is_async === true && is_trainer_match === false && ghost?.owner_user_id && ghost.owner_user_id !== userId` guard: read the owner's current pending row, push a new summary entry `{ match_id, challenged_at, challenger_anon_handle: generateAnonHandle(userId), subject, outcome, elo_delta }` where outcome is `ghost_won | ghost_lost | draw`, FIFO-cap the array at 50, sum `pending_elo_change += ghostOwnerEloDelta`, increment `pending_wins/losses/draws` based on outcome, write back with service-role. Buffer-write failures are logged but NEVER fail the live `/complete` response (losing one delta is fine; failing the live player's flow is not). **New endpoint `app/api/arena/v2/ghost-elo-summary/route.ts` GET.** `requireAuth` + `isArenaV2Enabled` gates; reads userId only from verified bearer; returns `{ pending: { elo_change, wins, losses, draws, summary, current_elo }, hasPending }`. `hasPending` is true iff `elo_change !== 0 || summary.length > 0` so a zero-delta-but-non-zero-W/L-D pile still triggers the card (rare edge from a perfectly-balanced run set). **New endpoint `app/api/arena/v2/claim-ghost-elo/route.ts` POST.** `requireAuth` + `isArenaV2Enabled` gates; userId from verified bearer (never body); idempotent (no-op response when buffer is already zero); reads snapshot, applies `arena_elo += pending_elo_change`, `arena_wins/losses/draws += pending_*`, then zeroes all 5 pending columns AND resets `pending_elo_summary` to `[]`. Returns `{ new_elo, wins_applied, losses_applied, draws_applied, elo_delta, noop }`. Known thin race window between read and write where a `/complete` write landing in the gap could be double-counted or lost; acceptable for Phase 3 (ms-scale window, rating-only impact, single match worst case). RPC-based atomic claim deferred to V1.5 if telemetry shows drift. **New component `components/arena-v2/GhostEloCard.tsx`.** SWR-backed (`useSWR("/api/arena/v2/ghost-elo-summary", swrFetcher, { revalidateOnFocus: true })`), renders NOTHING while loading or when `hasPending === false` so the lobby looks unchanged for the 95% case. When pending: glassmorphism card with purple-to-gold gradient background + 1px purple border + radial-glow accent in the corner + framer-motion fade-in respecting `prefers-reduced-motion`; "GHOST DUELS · WHILE YOU WERE OUT" tagline pill; bebas-font headline "Your ghost ran N duels" (pluralized); W/L/D stat row with green/red/purple color-coding; current to new ELO transition row with color-coded delta pill (green positive, red negative, purple zero); gold-gradient "Claim ELO" button. Claim calls `apiPost("/api/arena/v2/claim-ghost-elo", {})`, optimistically mutates SWR cache to the empty shape (so the card unmounts immediately), shows `toastSuccess` with the applied delta + new rating. Failure shows `toastError`. **Wire-in `app/arena/v2/page.tsx`.** Imported and rendered `<GhostEloCard />` at the top of the `phase === "lobby"` render block right after the hero/header section (inside the existing animate-slide-up wrapper). No other surfaces — scoped to V2 arena entry per Sam's directive. **Retune `scripts/seed-trainer-ninny-ghosts.ts`.** BANDS accuracy 75/85/95 to 60/75/90 with updated doc-comment explaining the cold-start friendliness intent. Added `--reseed` CLI flag (`RESEED = process.argv.includes("--reseed")`) that DELETEs all rows matching `owner_user_id = TRAINER_NINNY_USER_ID AND is_trainer = true` before inserting; default behavior (no flag) remains idempotent-skip. Idempotency note added warning that re-runs without `--reseed` will NOT update existing rows after an accuracy change. **Executed reseed** via `set -a && source .env.local && set +a && npx tsx scripts/seed-trainer-ninny-ghosts.ts --reseed`: 24 existing ghosts deleted, 24 reseeded (4 subjects × 3 bands × 2 ghosts; earth-science skipped at 0 questions in pool, same as Phase 1). **Verification SQL** `SELECT subject, elo_at_recording, total_score FROM duel_ghosts WHERE is_trainer = true ORDER BY subject, elo_at_recording;` returned 24 rows with avg `total_score` per band: 563 / 713 / 863 — matches new accuracy bands within mulberry32 sampling variance (theoretical: 600 / 750 / 900 for 10 questions at 60/75/90%). **Self-checks performed in-session:** `data-economist` lens — confirmed symmetric +/- math conserves the pool (live K=32 update mirrored on ghost owner), confirmed 60/75/90% doesn't interact with Fang flow (trainer matches still zero Fang transfer), confirmed 50-entry FIFO cap is sufficient (P99 of "matches against one user's ghost in 24h" expected <10 in early V2; 50 covers ~5 days of absence). `security-auth-guardian` lens — `requireAuth` on both new endpoints; both endpoints read userId from verified bearer only, never from body (claim-ghost-elo would otherwise let an attacker drain any user's buffer); idempotent zero-out cannot grant arbitrary ELO (second call returns noop without changing the row). **Copy compliance:** no em-dashes in user-facing strings (card headline, button label, toast bodies); "ELO" + "Wins/Losses/Draws" only (no "Wager"/"Winnings"); Fangs unaffected (this is rating-only). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean across the whole repo. Localhost test route: http://localhost:3000/arena/v2 (NEXT_PUBLIC_ARENA_V2_ENABLED must be true; otherwise client redirects to /arena). To manually test the card render: set `pending_elo_change = 12` + a synthetic summary entry on Sam's profile row via SQL, reload `/arena/v2`, card appears above subject picker, click Claim, arena_elo += 12, buffer zeroed, toast fires. **Deferred to Phase 4 / V1.5:** RPC-based atomic claim transaction to eliminate the thin read-then-write race window; telemetry build-out (weekly avg ELO drift detector, win/loss split by live-vs-live / live-vs-real-ghost / live-vs-trainer, distribution of `pending_elo_change` deltas at login, active player count per ELO band — `data-analytics` task pre-V2-public-launch); notification surface outside the V2 lobby (e.g. global nav dot when buffer non-empty) — scoped to V2 arena entry per Sam. Chain (this session): `admin` (orchestration) -> `dev-database` (migration 050 + 5 columns + applied to remote) -> `dev-backend` (complete-route patch + 2 new endpoints + service-role writes only) -> `data-economist` (self-check symmetric math + accuracy band + summary-cap sizing) -> `security-auth-guardian` (self-check auth surface + body-trust audit + idempotency review) -> `design-ui-ux` (GhostEloCard glassmorphism + radial-glow + transition layout spec) -> `dev-frontend` (GhostEloCard implementation + page wire-in + SWR cache mutation) -> `quality-code-reviewer` (typecheck clean, diff reviewed) -> `quality-docs-writer` (this entry + FEATURES + IOS_PARITY row + vault Daily/2026-05-26.md). iOS: paused per CEO web-only scope; IOS_PARITY row extended with Phase 3 status.

V1 Arena at `/arena` untouched. **New route `app/arena/v2/page.tsx`** is the full V2 experience: lobby with subject chip set (Algebra, Biology, Chemistry, Physics, Earth Science, Surprise Me — `surprise-me` randomly resolves to one of the five real subjects at queue time so the matcher gets a concrete subject), stake picker `[10, 25, 50, 100]` plus `250` gated at `arena_elo >= 1500`, Fangs balance + ELO header, atmospheric purple/blue/gold glows. After consent → 1.5s "Searching..." shimmer with min-floor → either no-ghost dead-end ("No challengers yet" + Notify Me opt-in stub) or 2.2s pre-match opponent reveal with TRAINER / MISMATCH / GHOST badge → battle. **Battle layout**: HP bars at top (`HpBar.tsx`, framer-motion spring fill, healthy-gold → warning-amber → danger-red → critical-pulse zones, prefers-reduced-motion respected, `role=progressbar` + `aria-valuenow`), emoji reactions left/right (`EmojiReaction.tsx`, unicode 😎/😅/😱/💀 with 😏 smug when opponent is more-dying — PNG-swap path reserved at `/public/arena-v2/emoji/` for V1.5), question text in glass card, MCQ grid (2 cols on sm+), live timer pill, COMEBACK ROUND badge + multiplier label on Qs 8/9/10. **Damage math**: correct = 10 base damage to opponent, wrong = 5 self-damage; speed scalar 1.0x → 1.5x by time-remaining ratio; combo multiplier `[1, 1.5, 2, 3]` cap 3x, stalls on wrong (does NOT reset, per spec); comeback Qs 8-10 are 1.5x flat on top of combo. Ghost replay poller hits `/api/arena/v2/ghost-replay` every 250ms, applies opponent damage at the recorded `time_ms` exactly once per question. **Live answers** reuse `/api/arena/answer` (V2 match is just `arena_matches` with `is_async=true` so the existing endpoint validates the live player). **Match complete** posts to `/api/arena/v2/complete`; results screen shows winner/loser headline + HP remaining grid + Fang delta + new ELO + loss-cap-reached note + shake-it-off +25F line (3-loss intervention full card deferred to 2B). **New components** under `components/arena-v2/`: `HpBar.tsx`, `EmojiReaction.tsx`, `ConsentModal.tsx` (locked copy, no em-dashes, ESC closes as decline, `aria-modal`), `GhostIdentity.tsx` (TRAINER blue-Ninny avatar + label, anonymized purple monogram circle otherwise; `viewerIsAdult` flag wired but force-anonymized in 2A because `profiles.birthdate` is not yet a column — adult opt-in unlock deferred to 2B). **New endpoint** `app/api/arena/v2/consent/route.ts` POST: hard-gated on `isArenaV2Enabled()`, idempotent (re-call on already-consented user returns existing state without re-writing), sets `ghost_consent_at` + `ghost_anon_handle` in one update; uses `requireAuth` (no body-trusted userId). **Copy stripped of em-dashes throughout** ("Real challengers unlock after 3 duels or 24h.", "We will not fake an opponent. When a real run lands, we will let you know.", "Got it, let's duel" / "Not now"). **String hygiene**: "Stake" not "Wager", "Prize" not "Winnings", Fangs icon via `cdnUrl("/F.png")`. **Deferred to Phase 2B (placeholders only — NOT built)**: 3-loss intervention card (backend returns `shakeItOffDispensed`; results shows a one-line placeholder), Mismatched-Duel full handicap UI (we just render halved stake), Settings → Privacy anonymity toggle + "Delete my ghost history" button, `profiles.birthdate` column + adult opt-in real-username gate, Privacy Policy + TOS 3-line copy delta, 2-layer audio, Pro perks (themes, replay export), Challenge Friend (button disabled with SOON hint). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. Localhost route: http://localhost:3000/arena/v2 (env must have `NEXT_PUBLIC_ARENA_V2_ENABLED=true`; otherwise client redirects to `/arena`). iOS: paused per CEO 2026-05-26 web-only scope.

- feat(web): **Arena V2 — Phase 1 backend foundation (staged, NOT committed, gated behind `NEXT_PUBLIC_ARENA_V2_ENABLED`).** Web-only scope per CEO override; iOS paused. V1 Arena keeps running unchanged. **Migration `lib/migrations/049_arena_v2_ghosts.sql`** adds the `duel_ghosts` table (id, owner_user_id with CASCADE, subject, elo_at_recording, question_ids uuid[], answers jsonb, total_score, recorded_at, is_trainer; RLS-enabled with owner-SELECT + non-owner-SELECT-for-matchmaking + service-role-only writes) plus new `profiles` columns (`ghost_consent_at`, `ghost_show_username`, `ghost_anon_handle`, `is_trainer_ninny`, `last_shake_it_off_at`) and `arena_matches` columns (`is_async`, `ghost_id` FK, `is_trainer_match`, `subject`). A deterministic Trainer Ninny system user is seeded at UUID `00000000-0000-0000-0000-00000000a155`. Range index `(subject, elo_at_recording, recorded_at DESC)` for the matcher cascade. **Helpers** at `lib/arena-v2/`: `feature-flag.ts` (NEXT_PUBLIC_ARENA_V2_ENABLED gate), `anon-handle.ts` (deterministic "Shadow Wolf 4729" handles via FNV-1a), `loss-cap.ts` (tier resolution -150/-300/-500/-1000 + 24h net-Fang query + 3-loss-streak counter), `ghost-matcher.ts` (subject-strict, ELO ±300, 24h then 7d expansion, Trainer-Ninny fallback for first 3 duels OR first 24h, mismatched-duel stake-halving flag, honest no-ghost dead-end). **Endpoints** at `app/api/arena/v2/` all hard-gate on `isArenaV2Enabled()` and return 404 when disabled: `queue/route.ts` POST (stake validation against 10/25/50/100 + 250-gated-at-ELO-1500, ghost-matcher dispatch, creates `arena_matches` row with `is_async=true` + `ghost_id` + `is_trainer_match`); `ghost-replay/route.ts` GET (returns `{answered, selected_index, time_ms, correct}` or `still_thinking` based on elapsedMs vs recorded time_ms — anti-cheat: never returns the question's correct_answer); `complete/route.ts` POST (atomic claim status='active' to 'completing', Qs8-10 1.5x comeback multiplier applied to points-not-stake, live-only ELO update with K=32, winner-takes-full-stake Fang transfer, **zero passive ghost-owner earn**, trainer-match Fang movement = 0, loss-cap enforcement stops further debit but never refunds, 3-loss-streak +25F shake-it-off dispense throttled to one per 24h via `profiles.last_shake_it_off_at`, lazy live-player ghost recording GATED on `profiles.ghost_consent_at IS NOT NULL`). **Seed script** `scripts/seed-trainer-ninny-ghosts.ts` is idempotent — 5 subjects times 3 ELO bands (1100/1400/1700) times 2 ghosts = 30 total, accuracy 75/85/95% per band, deterministic mulberry32 RNG per (subject, elo, slot) so re-runs are stable. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No UI work in Phase 1 — HP bar, consent modal, emoji reactions, 3-loss intervention card all ship in Phase 2. iOS: paused per CEO 2026-05-26 web-only scope; resume when Sam re-greenlights iOS.

- fix(web): **Streak ticked on UTC midnight + residual /dashboard hydration mismatch (local commit).** Sam reported the modal showed `DAY 2 STREAK!` after finishing only day 1, and the prior SwrProvider mount-gate (commit `292d899`) left a residual `<div> in <div>` mismatch on `/dashboard`. **Streak math** in `app/api/save-quiz-results/route.ts` and `lib/db.ts::upsertDailyActivity` was UTC-calendar-based: it incremented as soon as the YYYY-MM-DD string flipped, so a user who studied at 8pm ET (midnight UTC) had their streak tick instantly. Now time-based: require >= 20h since `last_activity_at` before incrementing, <= 48h to extend, <= 60h with a Streak Shield. Symmetric with the existing 36h expiry window. No schema change. **Hydration**: `app/dashboard/page.tsx` mount-gates the `statsReady && streak >= 3` fire-pill — the only conditional inside the ProtectedRoute-passed tree that branched on client-only SWR data. **Copy sweep**: scrubbed em-dashes from streak modal strings (`components/Navbar.tsx` lines 766, 770, 816, 850). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. iOS: 🟡 mirror-needed — iOS quiz/mastery save paths use the same UTC-day-rollover convention via the shared backend; the web-side fix above lands automatically because iOS calls the same routes. No iOS-only client work required.
- fix(ai): **MCQ answer-position de-bias across every game mode (commit `6212f57`, local, NOT pushed).** Follow-up to `5bd6445` which fixed only the Ninny generation path. Sam reported that Quiz, Mastery, and Arena were still landing answers on A or B almost every round. This commit closes the remaining surfaces at the source-of-bias layer. `lib/mastery-content.ts:391` prompt example flipped from `correctIndex: 0` to a position-2 example plus an explicit distribute-evenly instruction. `scripts/auto-generate-questions.ts` had its `"correct_answer": "A"` prompt example replaced with a positional-neutral "Third option" example, gained the same distribute-evenly instruction, and now Fisher-Yates-shuffles every row through a `shuffleRawQuestion` helper before both the on-disk JSON write and the DB upsert. `scripts/seed-questions.ts` and `scripts/seed-science.ts` each gained a Fisher-Yates `shuffleQuestionOptions` helper applied to every question read from source JSON before computing the `correct_answer` index for insert. Verification across every shuffle point shows ~25/25/25/25 ± noise. **Live DB tally** per vault Daily/2026-05-26 (this number comes from the previous admin run that performed a one-shot rewrite of existing rows before being stopped, so the live DB itself is also balanced): `questions` table went from A=33.7%/B=40.4%/C=19.5%/D=6.4% to A=24.9%/B=25.0%/C=24.8%/D=25.4%; `mastery_questions` went from A=32.4%/B=22.9%/C=21.2%/D=23.5% to A=25.7%/B=25.7%/C=22.9%/D=25.7%. Read paths (`lib/db.ts::getQuizQuestions`, `lib/question-bank.ts::getApprovedQuestions`, Arena match GET) were deliberately NOT shuffled at the read layer because server-side validation reads `correct_answer`/`correct_index` from the same stored row that backed the client read; shuffling on read without persisting would desync the validation. iOS: ✅ via-backend (calls same `/api/quiz`, `/api/arena/*`, `/api/mastery/*`, `/api/daily-drill` endpoints that read the same rebalanced rows; no iOS code change). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. Zero em-dashes added.

- fix(web): **Hydration mismatch on persisted SWR provider (local commit, NOT pushed).** Blocking-bug fix on commits `3111969`, `089aa9c`, `5bd6445`, `f185fba`. After Phase B's localStorage-persisted SWR cache landed, both `/dashboard` and `/quiz?subject=Science` started throwing `Did not expect server HTML to contain a <div> in <div>` on every refresh for signed-in users with a populated cache. Root cause: `lib/swr-config.ts:getProvider()` constructed the persisted provider on the very first render in BOTH environments. Server SSR has no localStorage so the cache initialized empty and the tree rendered the loading skeleton. The client's first render (the hydration commit) ran the same factory but the synchronous localStorage read populated the cache before useSWR hooks read it, so the client tried to paint the data DOM. Server tree != client first-render tree, React threw. **Fix (Option A — mount-gated SWRConfig).** `components/SwrProvider.tsx` now starts with `swrConfigNoPersist` (the plain in-memory variant added in `lib/swr-config.ts`) for the server render AND the client's hydration commit, then flips to the persisted `swrConfig` in a post-mount `useEffect`. The no-persist config mirrors every revalidation/retry setting so the only observable difference across the swap is whether the provider hydrates from disk. Trade-off: SWR cache is re-mounted across the swap so hooks may fire one extra revalidation immediately after hydration. Acceptable to keep server/client DOM aligned. **Why Option A and not Option B (deferred hydration in the shared factory).** The shared `createPersistedSwrProvider` in `packages/lionade-core/src/cache/storage.ts` already does hydration asynchronously (via an internal async IIFE that resolves `readyPromise`), but the localStorage read still resolves on a microtask which races with React's hydration commit. Solving this at the factory layer would require an opt-in `skipInitialHydration` flag plus a web-side `.hydrate()` call from `useEffect`, which touches the shared package and adds API surface. Option A keeps the entire fix inside web with zero change to the shared factory or to iOS, and the cost is one extra revalidation wave right after first paint. **Hard constraints respected.** No edits to `lib/auth.tsx`, `lib/supabase.ts`, or `middleware.ts`. No em-dashes in any user-facing copy. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. Localhost hard-refresh on `/dashboard` AND `/quiz?subject=Science` (signed in, populated localStorage) confirmed the hydration error gone in both. iOS: 🚫 N/A — React Native has no SSR so the hydration-mismatch class of bugs does not exist on iOS; the shared factory's existing `readyPromise` gate continues to serve iOS unchanged.

- feat(web): **Quiz Missions & Bet Float (V1)**, commit `3111969`. New floating pill button on `/quiz` that opens a bottom sheet showing Today's Missions and the active Daily Bet with **live-updating progress** as the user answers questions, so a player can keep working through the quiz flow without losing visibility into the rewards they are pacing toward. Sam's design call: the pill matches the existing `FocusMusic` / `QuickNote` / `LockIn` float family (bottom-right cluster, same idle-attention dim treatment, same Fang-iconography), the sheet uses a reusable framer-motion primitive, and **the float is not pinnable in V1** (open-and-close only; pinning is deferred to V2 as a follow-up).
  - **New components.** `components/Quiz/MissionsBetFloat.tsx` (the pill + sheet content; mounted by `app/quiz/page.tsx` only while `phase === "quiz"` so it never appears on the difficulty picker or results screens) and `components/ui/BottomSheet.tsx` (reusable framer-motion sheet primitive with Esc dismiss, click-outside dismiss, swipe-down-to-dismiss, focus-trap, ARIA modal role, and a `prefers-reduced-motion: no-preference` gate so the slide-up collapses to a fade for reduce-motion users).
  - **Hook surface.** `lib/hooks.ts` gained `useDailyMissions(uid)`, `useActiveBet(uid)`, and the exported `DailyMission` type. Cache keys are `dashboard-missions/${uid}` and `dashboard-active-bet/${uid}` so the Dashboard and the Quiz Float share one SWR cache; the Dashboard rewrite in `app/dashboard/page.tsx` consumes the same hooks and there are zero net new fetches.
  - **Live ticks.** `app/quiz/page.tsx` calls `mutate("dashboard-missions/${uid}")` and the matching active-bet key after every successful `handleSelect`, so the pill's badge count and the sheet's progress bars update in real time as the player answers. The pill briefly scale/glow-pulses when any mission's progress ticks up (also gated on `prefers-reduced-motion`).
  - **Cache-invalidation aliases.** `lib/cache-invalidation.ts` registers web aliases for `dashboard-missions/*` and `dashboard-active-bet/*` so existing top-level invalidators (purchase, equip, daily-spin payout, etc.) also bust these keys in the rare cross-flow case.
  - **Bundle delta.** Per `dev-frontend`'s build report, roughly 0.5 to 1 kB added to the `/quiz` route gzipped (framer-motion was already on the route, the new primitive + the float component are the only deltas; the BottomSheet primitive is reusable for future floats so the marginal cost amortizes).
  - **Deferred to V2.** Pinning the float so it stays open across questions, optional condensed inline progress on the float itself (without opening the sheet), and a "celebrate on completion" micro-interaction when a mission ticks to 100%. None of these block V1.
  - **iOS impact:** pending-port (yellow). Sam is paused on iOS builds for the rest of this session. iOS quiz screen would want this same surface; port plan is to mirror `MissionsBetFloat.tsx` to `components/Quiz/MissionsBetFloat.tsx` on iOS, with the BottomSheet primitive backed by `@gorhom/bottom-sheet` (already an iOS dep). Tracked in `IOS_PARITY.md` 2026-05-26 row.

## 2026-05-25 (Phase 1.5 — email program fully wired)
- feat(emails): **Email program Phase 1.5 (local commit, NOT pushed).** Closes the welcome-email wiring that Phase 1 deferred + audits every existing send-trigger for timing correctness + corrects the mastery-start gate to per-subject. End-to-end the email program is now fully wired and replay-safe; Sam pushes when ready. **(1) Welcome email wired via Supabase Auth webhook.** New route `app/api/auth/welcome/route.ts` accepts Supabase's post-verify hook, validates the bearer secret (`SUPABASE_AUTH_HOOK_SECRET` env var, constant-time compare, failure-closed if missing), looks up the user via `supabaseAdmin.auth.admin.getUserById(userId)` (recipient NEVER trusts the payload email — only the userId is used as a lookup key), idempotency-gates on `profiles.welcome_email_sent_at`, renders the Phase 1 `welcome` template, sends via Resend, then stamps the column with `.is("welcome_email_sent_at", null)` belt-and-braces so a concurrent retry never double-sends. On Resend failure the column stays NULL → Supabase retries → next attempt sends. On 401 (bad secret) Supabase retries with backoff. Path traversal / SQL injection / XSS surface audited clean (userId is parameterized; no HTML interpolation of payload data into email body). Rate-limited via the existing `/api/` catch-all in `middleware.ts` (100/min/IP — Supabase webhook traffic is well below this). **(2) Migration 048 — `welcome_email_sent_at timestamptz`** added to `profiles` with a partial index on `(id) WHERE welcome_email_sent_at IS NULL` for any future "who hasn't been welcomed yet" admin query. No backfill — existing pre-2026-05-25 accounts will NOT get a retroactive welcome (sending a "welcome" to someone using the app for weeks is worse than silence). Migration **NOT applied to prod** — Sam batches with the next push window per migration 047 precedent. RLS unchanged (profiles already has RLS from migration 001; welcome route writes via service role). **(3) Mastery-start gate corrected from per-user to per-exam.** Phase 1 wired the gate as "first mastery_sessions row across ALL exams" — meaning a user who starts AWS Sec then later Biology would only get one email ever. Sam's actual intent ("emails for like congrats on starting ur mastery on whatever subjects") is per-subject. Gate in `app/api/mastery/exams/[id]/sessions/route.ts` now filters by `(user_id, user_exam_id)` and the new exam triggers a new email; a second session on the SAME exam (manual fresh start, not resume — resume returns early upstream) does NOT re-trigger. **(4) Audit of the 4 existing wired triggers — all clean.** Waitlist (`app/api/waitlist/route.ts`): email fires AFTER successful insert, duplicate signup short-circuits with 409 BEFORE the email block (idempotent), Resend failure logged not thrown (best-effort, API still 200s). Contact form (`app/api/contact/route.ts`): subject embeds category + subject + sender email for triage, reply-to is the form-submitter; Resend failure DOES 500 the form (intentional — there's no DB row, a silent success would lose Sam's message entirely; documented as the safer-than-alternative tradeoff). First-streak-day (`app/api/save-quiz-results/route.ts`): gate `(profile.max_streak ?? 0) === 0 && newStreak === 1` reads BEFORE the streak UPDATE; second quiz same day sees max_streak=1 → no duplicate; midnight rollover from day 1 to day 2 sees max_streak=1 → no false fire; truly new user lands `0 → 1`, fires. Mastery-start: see (3). **(5) `lib/emails/supabase/README.md` updated** with both the 3-template paste steps AND a new §2 documenting the webhook URL + env-var + dashboard configuration + end-to-end test. **(6) `lib/emails/README.md` updated** — welcome row flipped from 🟡 deferred to ✅ wired with route + migration references. **(7) Welcome template doc-comment updated** to reflect Phase 1.5 wiring. **Subject lines** fit iOS Mail preview cut-off (~40 chars): "you're in." (10), "day 1. you're cooking." (22), "mastery: {subjectName}. locked in." (e.g. "mastery: AWS Sec Specialty. locked in." = 37), "welcome to lionade, {userName}." (varies, ~30 typical), contact-form subjects are Sam-facing triage so length is less critical. **CTA links** use `absoluteUrl()` from `lib/site-config.ts` (reads `NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL` with prod fallback) — no hardcoded `getlionade.com`. **No personal info in subject lines** except the contact form (intentional — Sam needs sender's email visible in his inbox for triage; the contact form is internal, not user-facing). **No new dependencies.** `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. `npx next build` clean (the new `/api/auth/welcome` route compiles + appears in build output). **No em-dashes or en-dashes in any user-facing strings** in the new route file or migration (grep clean on response bodies + UI strings; code comments retain dashes per the existing standing-order interpretation — only user-facing copy is dash-free). **Paste steps Sam still owes for full prod activation:** (a) 3 Supabase Auth Email Templates from `lib/emails/supabase/*.html`, (b) 1 webhook URL + bearer secret in Auth Hooks dashboard, (c) `SUPABASE_AUTH_HOOK_SECRET` env var on Vercel, (d) apply migration 048 to prod. All four steps are documented in `lib/emails/supabase/README.md`. Chain: admin (this autonomous run) → dev-backend lens (route handler audit of all 4 wired triggers + new welcome route design) → product-strategist lens (confirmed per-subject mastery-start intent from Sam's natural-language directive) → dev-database lens (migration 048 + partial index) → security-auth-guardian lens (constant-time bearer compare, server-side userId→email lookup, no cross-user leak, failure-closed on missing secret) → security-auditor lens (no SQL/XSS/path-traversal surface; payload userId parameterized; no payload-email trust) → security-rate-limiter lens (existing `/api/` catch-all at 100/min/IP sufficient — Supabase webhook traffic is well below) → quality-qa-tester lens (5-trigger dry-run: waitlist insert + duplicate; contact send success + Resend-failure tradeoff; first-streak transition + replay; mastery first-per-subject + second-same-subject + first-second-subject; welcome verify + replay-204 + bad-secret-401 + missing-secret-401 + Resend-fail-500-no-stamp + payload-missing-userid-200-skip + profile-missing-200-skip) → quality-code-reviewer lens (typecheck + build clean, naming consistent with existing routes, error JSON shapes match conventions). iOS: 🚫 N/A continuation of the 2026-05-25 Phase 1 row — emails are web backend infra reaching iOS users automatically.

- perf(web): **Data-loading Phase D — DEFERRED (no code change, CEO decision after admin halted on architectural blocker).** `dev-frontend` audit of `app/dashboard/page.tsx` (1279 LOC, 14 SWR hooks) found that 12 of 14 hooks are uid-scoped and require the user session, but Lionade has no cookie-based Supabase auth — session lives in `localStorage` (key `lionade-auth`) and API routes auth via `Authorization: Bearer` header. Zero hits for `@supabase/ssr`, `createServerClient`, or `cookies()` in the repo. A Server Component cannot read localStorage, so the spec'd Phase D (RSC + `Promise.all` server pre-fetch + `fallbackData`) is impossible without migrating auth to cookie-based SSR — which requires editing `lib/auth.tsx`, `lib/supabase.ts`, and `middleware.ts`, all on the **Do-Not-Touch list**. admin presented three options to CEO: (1) approve scoped exception for cookie-auth migration; (2) defer Phase D, ship A+B+C; (3) ship Phase D-lite (pre-fetch only the 2 anonymous hooks, ~14% of spec benefit). Sam chose (2). **No files modified, no commits, no dependency installs.** Phase D is filed as future work — when revisited, it requires its own dedicated session with `security-auth-guardian` involved from the start; the cookie-auth migration is the single highest-risk change in the codebase (breaks every authenticated page if done wrong). iOS impact: none (Phase D was always web-only by design — RSC doesn't exist in React Native; iOS cold-start was already addressed by Phase B's AsyncStorage hydration gate). The 4-phase data-loading sprint closes as **A+B+C shipped, D + C.1 + sign-out cache clear filed as future work.**

- perf(web): **Data-loading Phase C — `getSubjectStats` Postgres aggregation (web only, local commit, NOT yet pushed; migration NOT yet applied to prod).** Replaces the client-side aggregator in `lib/db.ts:614 getSubjectStats` with a single Postgres GROUP BY via the new `get_subject_stats(p_user_id uuid, p_lifetime boolean)` RPC. Old path SELECT'd up to 500 rows (5000 for the Profile lifetime variant) just to SUM() per-subject in JS — payload was ~95-98% wasted and the round-trip + JS loop was ~150-300ms per Dashboard load (and ~300-600ms on the Profile lifetime call). New path returns ~5-20 rows (one per subject) at ~5-20ms.
  - **Migration** — `lib/migrations/047_subject_stats_rpc.sql` creates the RPC. `CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION`, `LANGUAGE sql`, `STABLE`, `SECURITY INVOKER` (default — relies on existing `quiz_sessions_owner` RLS policy `auth.uid() = user_id`; we explicitly DO NOT use `SECURITY DEFINER` since the function takes `p_user_id` and DEFINER would be an RLS bypass). `SET search_path = public` to prevent schema-poisoning. `REVOKE FROM PUBLIC` + `GRANT EXECUTE TO authenticated, service_role`. Return columns are quoted camelCase (`"questionsAnswered"`, `"correctAnswers"`, `"coinsEarned"`) so the `.rpc()` result lands in the exact existing JS shape with zero field mapping needed on the client. Idempotent — safe to re-run.
  - **Index coverage** — `idx_quiz_sessions_user_completed (user_id, completed_at DESC)` from migration 039 already covers both the windowed (`completed_at >= now() - 90d`) and the lifetime variants (user_id prefix). No new index needed.
  - **`lib/db.ts` rewrite** — `getSubjectStats` is now a thin wrapper around `supabase.rpc("get_subject_stats", { p_user_id, p_lifetime })`. Return type explicitly annotated as `{ subject; questionsAnswered; correctAnswers; coinsEarned }[]` so callers (`app/profile/page.tsx`, `app/quiz/page.tsx`, `lib/hooks.ts:useSubjectStats`) get the same inferred shape. **Cache key in `lib/hooks.ts:useSubjectStats` (`subject-stats/${userId}/${lifetime}`) is unchanged** — Phase B's persisted SWR cache continues to hit transparently.
  - **Caller-side audit** — three consumers: `app/profile/page.tsx:166` (lifetime variant), `app/quiz/page.tsx:288` (windowed), `lib/hooks.ts:227 useSubjectStats` (both via opts). All consume the typed shape; no consumer touched.
  - **Type generation** — `@lionade/core/types/supabase.ts` does NOT yet include the new RPC because migration 047 is not on prod. After Sam pushes A+B+C and the migration applies, regenerate via Supabase CLI / MCP `generate_typescript_types` and commit. Until then, the RPC call is typed via the inline cast in `lib/db.ts:getSubjectStats`. Flagged in the docstring + iOS handoff.
  - **iOS handoff** — Phase C section appended to `packages/lionade-core/PHASE_B_NOTES.md` documenting the RPC name + exact signature + return shape + recommendation that iOS migrate via `ios-shared-core` adding a `subjectStatsAPI` wrapper to the shared package and ship in the same push window. Until prod has the migration, iOS can stay on its existing SELECT-and-aggregate path (`lib/hooks/use-subject-stats.ts` per the parallel iOS audit) — one-line internal swap once the RPC is live.
  - **Scope discipline** — flagged but NOT migrated this pass: `getBestScores (lib/db.ts:750)` is the same pattern (SELECT 500 + JS max per subject — would save ~100ms); `getRecentTopics (lib/db.ts:664)` is a 2-query design that could become one LATERAL RPC for ~30-50ms more. Both filed in `PHASE_B_NOTES.md` for a possible Phase C.2. `getQuizHistory` is pagination not aggregation — leave as-is.
  - **Quality gates:** `npx tsc --noEmit` clean (0 errors). Migration validated by hand (no Supabase branch run — Sam wants A+B+C local-only until the push window). `quality-qa-tester` dry-run on edge cases: zero-session user → `[]` (identical to old behavior), all-sessions-stale-in-windowed → `[]`, RLS-denied request (someone else's userId) → `[]`. NOTE: the old code had a 500/5000 row cap as a workaround for client-aggregate cost; the RPC has no cap (aggregation is server-side scan-once). For a hypothetical user with 10,000 sessions in 90 days, the RPC will be MORE accurate, not less. `dev-performance`: estimated 140-280ms saved per Dashboard load, 300-600ms per Profile load, ~95-98% network payload reduction. `security-auditor` signed off on `SECURITY INVOKER` + `REVOKE/GRANT` + `search_path` hardening — no RLS bypass surface. `quality-code-reviewer` clean — no "Do Not Touch" file modified, Phase A + Phase B diffs untouched, additive only.
  - **Status:** local commit only — **NOT yet pushed; migration NOT yet applied to prod**. Sam batches Phase A + B + C into one push window.

- perf(web): **SWR cache + tab-switch refetch fix — Phase B (web only, local commit, not yet pushed).** Builds on Phase A by formalising the cache-key registry as the shared cross-platform source-of-truth, and consuming the new `@lionade/core/cache/storage` factory + `StorageAdapter` interface that `ios-shared-core` shipped earlier the same day. Both web and iOS now run on the SAME `createPersistedSwrProvider` scaffold; only the platform-specific I/O adapter differs.
  - **Hook migration to shared `cacheKeys` registry** — `lib/hooks.ts`: `useUserStats` + `mutateUserStats` now consume `cacheKeys.userStats(userId)` from `@lionade/core/cache/keys` instead of inline template strings. Same string output (`user-stats/${userId}`) so no cache invalidation; sourced from the canonical helper so any future shape change is a one-line edit in the shared package, mirrored on iOS automatically. Hook count migrated this pass: **1** (useUserStats) — the only hook whose inline key matched a registry helper string exactly. Remaining 26 useSWR sites have key drift vs registry (different naming, missing limit/lifetime params, dashboard-page-local hydrators) — each one documented in `packages/lionade-core/PHASE_B_NOTES.md §2` with a proposed registry extension for `ios-shared-core` to ship. Web migrates the moment each helper exists.
  - **Shared persistence factory consumed** — `lib/swr-config.ts` no longer reimplements hydrate/persist/debounce/LRU; it calls `createPersistedSwrProvider(adapter, opts)` from `@lionade/core/cache/storage`. The shared factory returns `{ cache, readyPromise, flush }`; web ignores `readyPromise` (localStorage is sync so cache is populated on first microtask) while iOS gates `SplashScreen.hideAsync()` on it. `flush()` is wired to the existing visibilitychange + beforeunload listeners. Net diff: `swr-config.ts` shrunk from 137 LOC to 134 LOC but with ALL the persistence semantics now shared cross-platform.
  - **Web localStorage adapter** — new file `lib/cache/localStorageAdapter.ts` (~100 LOC, web-internal, NOT in shared package). Pure I/O surface: 4 promise-typed methods wrapping `window.localStorage` with SSR guards + quota-swallow. Also exposes `stripSkippedKeys()` which `swr-config.ts` applies to the persisted JSON blob right before write.
  - **Persist-skip list** — explicit list of SWR key prefixes that stay in-memory only (no localStorage round-trip). Skipped: `leaderboard-*` (200-row payloads, revalidate every 30s anyway), `social-feed/*` (large feed blobs), `dashboard-weekly-chart/*` (rich UI-state-coupled chart), `mastery-session/*` (session-bound, short-lived). In-memory SWR cache still holds them for the page lifecycle. Applied at the adapter boundary (`withSkipList` wrapper in `swr-config.ts`) so the policy stays platform-local — the shared factory has no concept of skip lists by design, leaving iOS free to define its own (or none).
  - **Cross-platform coordination doc** — `packages/lionade-core/PHASE_B_NOTES.md` updated by admin (web) after consuming the iOS-shipped interface: 9 specific key-drift items needing shared `cacheKeys` helpers, persist-skip-list reasoning, sign-out cache-clear open question (`lib/auth.tsx` is "Do Not Touch" — CEO sign-off required to wire), versioning protocol. Web does NOT edit shared-package source — admin consumes, iOS team owns.
  - **iOS shared interface arrival:** `ios-shared-core` shipped `@lionade/core/cache/storage.ts` (interface + factory) the same day, in parallel with web's adapter work. Web pivoted from a local interface mirror to the canonical import as soon as the file landed — zero waste, clean consume.
  - **Quality gates:** `npx tsc --noEmit` clean (0 errors). `npm run core:typecheck` clean. `quality-qa-tester` walked happy path + 5 edge cases (cold load empty localStorage, cold load full localStorage, tab-switch warm load, signed-out → signed-in transition, localStorage quota error) — all pass. `quality-code-reviewer` clean — no "Do Not Touch" files modified, `keepPreviousData` preserved globally, Phase A `revalidateOnFocus` keep-list untouched. `dev-performance` confirmed: skip-list reduces visibilitychange persist payload by ~20–30% (rough estimate from typical leaderboard + feed sizes); no new network calls; bundle delta negligible — the factory module is small + tree-shaken into the same chunk as `swr-config.ts`.
  - **Status:** local commit only — **NOT yet pushed**. Sam reviews before push.

- perf(web): **SWR cache + tab-switch refetch fix — Phase A (web only, local commit, not yet pushed).** Surgical 5-change pass that eliminates the per-tab-switch revalidation storm against Supabase / `/api/*`. Audit found tab-switching between Dashboard ↔ Shop ↔ Compete ↔ Academia was firing a full revalidation cascade on every focus event (every page) plus a `POST /api/bounties/rotate` on every dashboard mount. After this pass: tab-switches read from cache (no network), per-hook overrides preserve the freshness-sensitive surfaces.
  - **Global SWR defaults flipped** — `lib/swr-config.ts`: `revalidateOnFocus: true → false`, `dedupingInterval: 5_000 → 60_000`. `keepPreviousData: true` retained so background revalidations never flash a skeleton. Hooks that materially need cross-tab freshness keep their per-hook `revalidateOnFocus: true` override (Navbar notifications, `useUserStats` Fangs balance, Social unread badges, ClockIn, StreakRevive, DailySpin, useStreakInfo, usePlan, useEloLeaderboard via dedupe, and ~20 page-level hooks that explicitly opt in — verified, all kept).
  - **Shop inventory raw `useEffect` → SWR** — `app/shop/page.tsx`: `loadInventory()` `useEffect` replaced with `useSWR("shop-inventory/" + user.id, ...)` (60s dedupe, keepPreviousData). `handlePurchase` + `handleEquip` now call `mutateInventory()` from the same key so equip/purchase still feels instant via post-mutation revalidate. Dropped unused `useCallback` import.
  - **Compete leaderboard raw `useEffect` → shared hook** — `app/compete/page.tsx`: replaced `useState + useEffect(getEloLeaderboard(5))` with `useEloLeaderboard(5)` (the existing `lib/hooks.ts` hook, 30s dedupe + shared cache with `/leaderboard` page). Removed dead `useState`/`useEffect` React imports.
  - **`/api/notifications` poll deduped between Navbar + Social** — `components/Navbar.tsx` + `app/social/page.tsx`: previously each page polled the endpoint on its own SWR key (`social-notifs/${uid}` on Social, raw `setInterval` on Navbar) → endpoint was hit twice every 15s when both were mounted. Both now keyed on `notifications/${user.id}` — single cache, single 15s poll, single realtime INSERT channel (Navbar's) invalidates the shared key so Social updates instantly. Navbar's optimistic local-state setters (mark-all-read) preserved by hydrating from SWR `onSuccess`.
  - **Dashboard bounty-rotation no longer auto-fires on every mount** — `app/dashboard/page.tsx`: `useEffect → POST /api/bounties/rotate` gated by `localStorage["bounties-last-rotation"]` 1h timestamp. Server still owns canonical rotation cadence; this is a client-side coalesce. (Long-term: move to Supabase cron — tracked separately.)
  - **Quality gates:** type-check passes (0 errors). `quality-qa-tester` signed off on tab-switch happy path + 4 edge cases (Fangs after purchase, Shop inventory after equip, Navbar/Social cache share, stale class list, stale Fangs after Daily Spin). `quality-code-reviewer` clean. Lint not run (no ESLint config wired; Next would scaffold interactively — skipped to avoid touching project config without Sam's consent — flagged for follow-up).
  - **Phase A retrofit — stripped redundant per-hook `revalidateOnFocus: true` overrides** (local commit, not yet pushed). The initial Phase A flipped the global default to `false` but left ~24 explicit per-hook `revalidateOnFocus: true` overrides untouched, so the global change was a no-op on those sites. This retrofit audited all 24 against Sam's confirmed keep-list (`useUserStats`, `useStreakInfo`, `usePlan`, Navbar+Social notifications, live mastery session) and stripped the override from 17 sites, keeping it on 7. Strips: `app/study-dna/page.tsx`, `app/classes/page.tsx`, `app/learn/mastery/page.tsx`, `app/learn/ninny/page.tsx`, `app/classes/[id]/page.tsx`, `app/academia/page.tsx` (×2), `app/dashboard/page.tsx` (YourClassesRow), `components/DailyDrillWidget.tsx`, `components/DailyReadyNudge.tsx`, `components/Class/SyllabusUpload.tsx`, `components/Class/GradeTracker.tsx`, `components/Class/ClassStreakChip.tsx`, `components/Class/FlashcardStudy.tsx`, plus 3 **borderline strips flagged for human review**: `components/ClockInButton.tsx`, `components/StreakReviveBanner.tsx`, `components/Shop/DailySpinHero.tsx` (all three still have `refreshInterval: 60_000` so freshness is preserved at minute granularity; Phase A swr-config comment had named them as keepers, but the confirmed keep-list did not). Type-check clean, QA re-validated, code review clean.
  - **Out of scope for Phase A (intentionally):** Dashboard RSC promotion (Phase D), `lib/db.ts:614 getSubjectStats` rewrite (Phase C), `@lionade/core` extraction (Phase B). No file in those scopes was touched.
  - **iOS impact:** iOS team is running an equivalent Phase A in parallel (different libraries — `useSWR` shape on iOS already exemplary per 2026-05-13 audit; iOS work targets its own focus-revalidate cadence). Cross-platform parity row added to `IOS_PARITY.md` covering "both platforms staged, awaiting user greenlight to push/build."
  - **Status:** local commit only — **NOT yet pushed**. Sam reviews staged commits before push.

  - **Claim button single-click claim** — `components/ClockInButton.tsx`: when the daily button is in the available-to-claim state, clicking it now claims **instantly without auto-opening** the history popover. The previous behavior was `claim() AND setOpen(o => !o)` unconditionally — the popover open was a friction step the user didn't want. Cooldown/claimed state still opens the popover on click (so the user can see the countdown + history). `aria-label` updated to reflect the conditional behavior.

Recorded in `IOS_PARITY.md`.

Not blockers.
